Atɛmmuo a ɛkɔɔ International Court of Arbitration hyɛɛ Ghana sɛ ɔmfa Ghana Sika boɔ yɛ deɛ ɛtoɔ a Early Termination Payment, together with Mobilization, Demobilization ne ɛbɛhwɛ ne maintenance costs wɔ US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduonu (Lion) 134,348,661, ne nsiho a ɛwɔ ho sɛ wapeperɛ no bɛtua sika no mu efiri 12 November 2018, berɛ a na ɛka no bɛtua sika no mu nto US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduonu(6%).
Ghana aban nso gyinaeɛ sɛ wɔde GPGC sika sidi mpem aduasa (US$ 309,877.74 wɔ akadeɛ a ɛto so) no mu, ne nnwɔtwe (€ 3,000,000) ne ɛtoho a wɔde rema GPGC rekasa ne nnwɔtwe a ɛkyerɛwɔ mu expert witness, ne nsiho a wɔde gu ɛka sika no ( US$ 3,309,877.74 wɔ ɛka a wɔde gu ɛtɔ so, LIBOR for three-month US dollar deposits, compounded quarterly.

Yei happened berɛ a Yawoada abatoɔ abɔ fam ase. Amanfoɔ kyerɛ sɛ, saa nneɛma yi yɛɛ ɛboaa ne gods.
Ɔmanfoɔ a ɛwɔ mpuntuo no de sika hyɛɛ ɔde agu hɔ na ɛbue ne mu.
Ɔne Kasapa FM Mfinimfi Mantam mu kasamafoɔ Yaw Boagyan, Wofa Yaw Obosu a ɔyɛ adwumakuo a ɔwɔ mantam no mu na ɔkaa sɛ, saa nhyehyɛeɛ asi ɛfiri sɛ wakɔɔ mantam no mu na ɔsanso deɛ ɛyɛ anika.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ wɔde nkrataa no bɛtɔn akɔ so wɔ mankessim, Kasoa, markets mu. “Sɛ saa nneɛma yi rekɔ so wɔ mansini no mu a, mitu aduanan a wɔbɔ mmɔden sɛ merekabɔ me no ayɛ adwuma wɔ Mankessim, Kasoa, markets mu.”
“Yei nyinaa mmõa firisɛ biribi saa a ɛte Ajumako Ochiso Community mu.”
Mprenpren mu no, nnipa a wɔbɔɔ kar ase mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmmubea hɔ no nso hyɛɛ Asoeɛ a ɛhɔ Fisheries ne Aquaculture sɛ wɔmfa wɔn mmoaboa wɔn mma wɔmfa mmoaboa a wɔde tu kar no akɔ nsesaeɛ.
“Yɛn nnwuma a yɛn ho hia wɔ Ajumako Ochiso Community mu ɛna yɛbɛtumi anya adwuma wɔ yɛn mma asuafoɔ ne household. Yɛreserɛ asoeɛ mu sɛ ɔmmra yɛn ho sɛ yɛbɛtumi ayɛ ɔhaw a ɛresi yɛn wɔ Ajumako Ochiso Community mu” a resident appealed.
Assembly Member a ɔdi kan wɔ Ajumako Ochiso South Maxwell Mensah nso hyɛɛ Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ Asoeɛ ne Aban ahodoɔ nnwumakuo ahodoɔ sɛ wɔmfa mmoa a ɛmma wɔn retu anamɔn na wɔanya mfasoɔ biara nni hɔ.
Executive Director for the Institute of Energy Security, Nana Amoasi VII, a ɔyɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin, Godfred Dame de n’ano kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɔmfa ne fa ato Ghana sika ɔpepepem ɔha aduoson a wɔnyaa power company, The Ghana Power Generation Company (GCGP) nsa.
Berɛ a ɔne Morning Starr rekasa Wukuada no, Nana Amoasi VII frɛɛ Attorney General sɛ ɔmfa Ghanafoɔ nhyehyɛeɛ nti ɔmfa ɔpepem ɔha aduoson ($170 million) no ho asɛm.
“Yɛbɛtumi ayɛ wɔn anim sɛ wɔbɛka asɛm yi gyinaeɛ nanso yɛpɛ sɛ yɛgyina Covid-19 ne abatoɔ asɛm yi nhyɛ excuses. Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ ne Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ nso nnyɛ papa. Ɔnhwɛ kwan na ɔnhwɛ yɛn ho bio. Ɔbɛtumi atena yɛn ho adi sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ yɛn ho bio.”
Asɛm yi asi wɔ Commercial Court a ɛwɔ London rejected a late appeal from Ghana against US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduoson a ɛyɛ power contractor, The Ghana Power Generation Company (GCGP) nsa.
London Kɔɔto Baatan no kyerɛɛ mu sɛ Ghana aban anwene sɛ wɔmfa afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu Ayɛwohomumɔ 26, 2021 decision a London-based United Nations Commission on International Trade Law (UNCITRAL) Tɛtɛɛtɔ so no.
Kɔɔto Baatan wɔ ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ biara Wukuada, Ayɛwohomumɔ 8, agyinaeɛ a Ghana aban anwene sɛ ɔbɛpɛ sɛ ɔbɛgye award no ho dwuma-a ɔde kaa ho sɛ ɔman no nnyinasoɔ a ɛwɔ sɛ ɔbɛgu award no ho dwuma yie.
Aban nam ne ɔbaa'adwumayɛfoɔ Godfred Dame anwene sɛ ɔnsosɔeɛ wɔ 2020 abatoɔ ne COVID-19 yadeɛ no nto ngu ɛna wɔnyɛ excusesɛm buaa London kɔɔto no.
GPGC dii kan wɔ asɛnnibea ano, Charles Kimmins QC ne Mark Tushingham gyinaa too mu sɛ, Ghana bɛkaa sɛ ɛyɛ too late sɛ wɔbɛsanhwɛ gyinaeɛ a wɔyɛɛ ho asɛm no mu.
Ghana de too dwa, Khawar Qureshi QC a ɛwɔ Serle Court ne Volterra Fietta firisɛ deɛ wɔn anim no, GPGC de too dwa, Kimathi & Partners de too dwa, na nnipa a wɔwɔ FTI Consulting no baeɛ.
Ghana nso wɔ ɔmanpanin adwumakuo no kɔɔto Amofa & Partners a wɔwɔ Nkran no.
John Beechey, a ɔyɛ International Criminal Court's Court of Arbitration ne co-chaired by Prof Albert Fiadjoe, a Ghanaian academic, wɔdii kan kɔɔ nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ a wɔhwɛ ama power producer ano ɔhyɛ US dollar ɔpepem aduonu ($170 million).
Out of the total, U dollar ɔpepem aduonu nsia ($134.35 million) gyinaeɛ sɛ ɛyɛ US dollar ɔpepem aduonu nsia ($69.36 million) sika a wɔde ahyɛ termination fee, US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduonu num (#58.49 million) sika a wɔde ahyɛ ɛfiri US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduonu num, US dollar ɔpepem mmeɛnsa ne US dollar ɔha ahanan.

Nteeɛ krataa a wɔyɛɛ asɛm yi ho no bi nom kyerɛɛ sɛ Ahenkora Committee a ɛhwɛ animtiakyire a wɔredi kɔɔto gyinaeɛ no nnyɛ sufficient groundsɛn sɛ wɔbɛsi gyinaeɛ a ɛda GPGC sika ɔpepepem ɛsiane sika dɔla no mpem aduowɔtwe($US 18 million).
Kɔɔto Baatan no de asɛm no mu ahwehwɛ Ghana asɛm no ho, na wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔtwa toɔ no ahyɛ aseɛ sɛ, ɛyɛ evidence nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔde agu akwan foforɔ a wɔfrɛ no Kpone-Katamanso aseɛ afe 15, 2017.

Wɔ British mmara no, na aban no wɔ nsakraeɛ a wɔde too atɛnmuafoɔ no gyinaeɛ. Nanso, ɛkɔɔ so no, wɔkɔ kɔɔto mmiɛnsa mma wɔn rekɔsi Kɔɔto no akyi dapɛn mma wɔn a wɔbɛsan kraeɛ no.

Yei yɛ saa berɛ yi, British mmaranimfoɔ Volterra Fietta hyɛɛ aban no sɛ ɔne wɔn ahyɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ no ase.

Ɔtemmuafoɔ a ɔtenaa adwuma no, Justice Butcher amfa ho mmuae.
Ɔkyerɛɛfoɔ no kaa sɛ aban de ketewa a ɛregu so no yɛ deɛ "significant and substantial" berɛ a sɛ wɔreba fam nsɛm a ɛtɔ so mmienu no aduasa nnwɔtwe a ɛtɔ so enum aduasa nnwɔtwe a edi kan no dɔɔso, na awieɛ dɔla a ɛtɔ so mmienu no awieɛ.

Akyinnyegyeɛ a ɛwɔ Atɛmmuo no ho

Atɛmmuo a ɛkɔɔ International Court of Arbitration hyɛɛ Ghana sɛ ɔmfa Ghana Sika boɔ yɛ deɛ ɛtoɔ a Early Termination Payment, together with Mobilization, Demobilization ne ɛbɛhwɛ ne maintenance costs wɔ US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduonu (Lion) 134,348,661, ne nsiho a ɛwɔ ho sɛ wapeperɛ no bɛtua sika no mu efiri 12 November 2018, berɛ a na ɛka no bɛtua sika no mu nto US dollar ɔpepem ɔha aduonu(6%).

Bere a nsu yiri faa ɔbabun bi wɔ Sawaba a ɛwɔ Kumasi following the Wukuada a osu kɛse wɔ Asante Mantam mu no.
Bere a abofra no rehyɛ n'awofo hyɛn mu wɔ tricycle mu bere a aberɛ a nsu yiri faa pon no mu yɛɛ den.
Amanfoɔ a wɔte mpɔtam hɔ kyerɛ sɛ ɛfiri ɔhaw no mu sɛ wɔbɛtumi de ayɛ amawofoɔ nanso ɔde n’awofoɔ no ankɔsisi n’awofoɔ asɛm no.
Ɔfoforɔ bi ka kyerɛɛ Francis Abba wɔ Morning Starr dwumadie so sɛ: “Sɛ nsu tɔ wo bo a, ɛnyɛ den sɛ wobenya no fɔ. Awofo no nnyaa nteaseɛ pii na ɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛduru Sawaba kwan no. Nsu no kɔ nwonwa so, enti yɛnnim ɛmfa baako a ɔwɔ no na ɛde gyinaeɛ kwan a ɛkɔɔ so a na yareɛ ama no ayɛ den kyerɛɛ yɛn.”
Nsɛm ahodoɔ a ɛka nso kyerɛ sɛ Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo a ɔwɔ Atifi Atɔeɛ mantam no nni nnyinasoɔ wɔ nsu no mu.
Asante Mantam mu Polisifo asoeɛ de too dwa sɛ, Iddrisu Adams alias Koomi a ɔyɛ Asante Mantam mu Polisifo asoeɛ de faa nsɛmmɔne bi wɔ berɛ a na korɔnobɔ ahodoɔ yi atwa ne ho ahyɛ polisifo ase sɛ ɔmma ɔmfa ne polisifo nsɛm mu.
Onipa a wɔyɛ mmonnaa yi wɔ asoafoɔ nhwehwɛmu na wɔakyere no Ayɛwohomumɔ 22nd, 2021, Polisifoɔ oprehyɛn so reyɛ adwuma.
Wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ bosome da a ɛtɔ so aduonu num wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe na ɔreyɛhunuu sɛnea ɔreyɛ kurow no mu aberɛ a polisifo no tuo no mmonnaa.
Wɔde no kɔɔ St. Martins Ayaresabea hɔ no a na ɔde wawu no.
Polisifoɔ a wɔde kaa polisifoɔ kyerɛɛ sɛ wɔn ani gye ne nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ a wɔhwɛ polisifoɔ akyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmfa ne mmoa mma wɔn a wɔmfa Polisi Station no ho.
Polisifoɔ nso hyɛɛ ɔmanfoɔ wɔ wɔn bɔ sɛ wɔn bɛko ama wɔn na wɔn nso yɛ bɔne ama wɔn cooperation.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ National Security ano, Albert Kan Dapaah aka nsɛm bi a ɔde forceful eviction of Ashanti Regional Security Coordinator DCOP Opare-Addo (rtd) a ɔyɛ National Securityfoɔ adwuma wɔ dwumadie no mu.
Kan Dapaah kyerɛɛ mu sɛ, saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi baa so berɛ a na ɔreyɛ adwuma no ama adwumayɛfoɔ a ɔhwɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ adwuma no futile.
Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔde too dwa no kyerɛɛ Starr News sɛ, na ɔPP awɔte group, Delta Force, assaulted no wɔ ɔkwan a na ɔnam so yi soboɔ sɛ ɔnhwɛ wɔn bidding wɔ ɔmantam no mu.
Nanso berɛ a ɔman security soafoɔ kyerɛɛ nsɛm a efi South Dayi MP Rockson-Nelson Dafeamekpo kyerɛɛ mu no, ɔman security soafoɔ no kyerɛɛ sɛ menfoɔ no yɛ national securityfoɔ.
Nanso ɔhyɛɛ m’adwene sɛ ɔnteeɛ nea mfasoɔ wɔ Owura Opare-Addo ananteɛ no sii gyinaeɛ sɛ ɔde force adwuma no ho dwuma.
“Ɔpare-Addo na wahyɛɛ asante mantam mu nsɛntwerɛfoɔ a wɔde bɛdi dwuma wɔ Asante mantam mu firi Kɔtɔnima bosome da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Yei yɛn foforɔ yi ahyɛɛ aseɛ Ayɛwohomumɔ da a ɛtɔ so nan wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Nnipa foforɔ yi ahyɛɛ aseɛ Ayɛwohomumɔ da a ɛtɔ so aduasa wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
Ɔyɛɛ saa nti na n’addo no antwerɛtwerɛ afe so Kɔtɔnima bosome da a ɛtɔ so aduonu nsia wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Berɛ a ɔtwerɛtwerɛ no reba no, DCOP Opare-Addo wɔahataeɛ maa Ashanti regional security nkabom krataa foforɔ no. Ɔsan de too dwa sɛ ɔde krataa foforɔ no bɛhyɛɛ Colonel Francis Arthur (rtd) sɛ ɔyɛ Asante regional security nkabom krataa foforɔ no afe yi Ayɛwohomumɔ bosome da a ɛtɔ so nan wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Nanso ɔpare-Addo am
Owura Dapaah kyerɛɛ mu sɛ “Nteaseɛ a wabɔ wɔn ho no, n’adwene a ɔrekɔ so wɔ dwumadie yi so ɛbɔ abasobɔ a ɔhwɛ nsrahwɛfoɔ wɔ mansini no mu. Against saa backdrop yi, personnel a ɔwɔ Asante mantam mu firi Kɔtɔnima bosome da a ɛtɔ so dunson wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Sɛ ɛbɛyɛ a nanso ɔhyɛɛ papa akyerɛ wɔn ho sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ ɔnhyɛn krataa a ɛwɔ ne dwumadie mu hɔ.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ “ani nyinaa ara, obiara a ɔhwɛ ma DCOP Opare-Addo sɛ ɔyɛ n’asoeɛ a ɔhwɛ ma national security coordinator anaa me sɛ ɔhwɛ mansini soafoɔ wɔ ɔnoara nnyinasoɔ a wɔde assault wɔ no ho. Neither wɔn soafoɔ a ɔhwɛ ma polisi nkorabata biara wɔ saa ntwasoɔ yi ara”
“Mɛpɛ sɛ yɛma fie hyɛ yɛn kwan sɛ yɛbɛhwehwɛ asɛm yi mu sɛ ɔnhwɛ ama DCOP Opare-Addo banbɔ biara.”

Ɔtɛmmɔn mu no, karkafoɔ a wɔtuo ne payloader dwumadie yi too hɔ ma Apolisifoɔ nanso ɔmmraa ne nnipa Klutse Kofi a na ɔyɛ Mitsubishi Pickup a wɔfrɛ no GE 7191-19.

Ɔkaa sɛ na saa na nnipa yi kyerɛɛ Polisi sɛ weapons no yɛ Sammertide Construction ne Sand Winning Company.

Ayɛwohomumɔ 15, 2021, bɛyɛ nɔn a na ɔreka agudeɛfoɔ Osae Kwame firi ne farm ayɛwohomumɔ kɔɔ Adeiso kuropɔn sɛ ɔbɛtɔ aduan ma ne farm labourers nan met the nnipa a wadi mfeɛ aduonu baako sɛ wɔwɔ pick-up vehicles ne Jeep a na ɛwɔ tu agudeɛ no GS 9835-19, stopped by him, handcuffed na abducted him into one of the Pick-Up vehicles na ɔde ɔno kɔɔ Tank Akuraa a farming community a ɛwɔ Adeiso.
Polisifoɔ wɔ ɔstress calls asɛm yi kyeree village na ɔbɔɔ ɔbaa no nanso nnipa a ɔwɔ kyɛfɛ no ara nadi sɛ ɔmmra saa nnipa yi tuo wɔɔ Obeng Yaw dwumadie a ɛwɔ Adeiso amidwen sporadic firing of gunshots.
Kwantenpɔn a ɛtɔ so mmienu yi Alhassan Zakari srɛɛ wɔn bɔɔ ne leg during a ɔmmra atuo no ano.
Wɔkyeree nnipa baanan a ɛboro mmienu yi wɔ fagudeɛtubea hɔ, na wɔnam so kɔkɔ wɔn kwan bi so.
Kwanyieni a ɔwɔ kwan no so gye too mu sɛ nnipa a wɔabɔ wɔn kwaadubɔ afiri hɔ no, na wɔhunuu sɛ nnipa bɔɔ Ghc 96,000 wɔ tuo gua no mu berɛ a na wɔretu fagudeɛ no.
Kyebi Polisifoɔ a wɔyɛ nnipa baanan yi kyeree wɔn a na ɔwɔ kyɛfa wɔ wireless message so no akyi.
Wɔ Adeiso Polisifoɔ nhwehwɛmu bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ yi kaa ho.
Nana Barfuor Sarpong a ɔyɛ Jeep bi a ɔda hɔ ne Nana Barfuor Sarpong a ɔka kyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔyɛ Polisifoɔ dwuma tetee bi ak47 a assault rifle, one pistol, ne mmeamme shell mmeɛnsa a na wɔahata Polisifoɔ baako.
Onipa a atoyerɛnkyɛm yi -Alhassan Zakaria ne Bright Apama a yaw no ara srɛɛ wɔn ho dwuma wɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu Bere a na wɔayɛ oprehyɛn wɔ Koforidua.
Atwereyɛ Mantam mu no, Ekuo a ɛwɔ Apueɛ Mantam no agye asɛm no so.
Nnipa a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ no bɔɔ Bail
Koforidua Circuit Court de nnipa baanan a ɔwɔ nnipa baanan akyi ne Akyem Abuakwa a ɔyɛ National Securityfoɔ dwumadie gyinaeɛ sɛ ɔwɔ ɔpepepem aduonu nan akyi.
Nnipa a ɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ yi ne Nana Barfuor Sarpong, Nana Barima Twum Tarbiade II, both sub-chiefs a ɔwɔ Akyem Abuakwa.
Restu yɛ Jonathan Martey,Eric Yaw Obeng,Victor Ahenkora Koranteng ne nkurɔfoɔ a wɔn large.
Wɔde wɔn asɛnnibea kɔɔto asɛnnibea wɔ Fiada, Ayɛwohomumɔ 18, 2021. Wɔde wɔn korɔnobɔ afa ɛsɛ sɛ; korɔnobɔ aponoɔ, Kidnapping, causing unlawful harm, stealing, conspiracy to commit robbery, robɔfoɔ ne ammunition
Asɛm no adjourned kɔɔ so Dwoada, Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu nson.
Kwaadubɔfoɔ Cyril Boateng Keteku, Assistant State Attorney kyerɛɛ kɔɔto no sɛ, ababaawa a ɔdi kan wɔ asɛm no mu no, Osae Kwame, 59, yɛ ɔmfrɛ, na ɔno a ɔdi kan no, Alhassan Zakari, 39, yɛ ɔmfrɛ.
Owura a ɔdi kan no Samuel Astu Forson ne Chief of Adeiso na ɔyɛ Executive Officer of Summertide sand winning Company.
Ɔkaa sɛ nnipa a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ yi ne Nana Baffuor Sarpong a ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔyɛ National Security Personnel a ɛhyɛ ma Fagudeɛ Asoeɛ sɛ ɔyɛ nteteeɛ Coordinator ne timber monitoring officer.
Ɔbaa a owura no akwaafoɔ Nana Barima Twum Tabirade kyerɛɛ sɛ ɔhwɛ Akyem landsi mu. Ɔbaa a owura no akwaafoɔ Jonathan Martey yɛ Nana Barfuor baanu, na ɔno a ɔno nso a owura no Victor Ahenkora Koranteng kyerɛɛ sɛ ɔyɛ Immigration Officer.
Abɔneyɛfoɔ a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ no nyinaa kɔɔ so
Aban abɔ ato hɔ sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ a atoyerɛnkyɛm a ɛfiri Burkinabe bɔne no so wɔ Ghana asɛm berɛ a ɔde barracks a ɛwɔ Bawku no sɛ ɔbɛboa banbɔ ho ban wɔ ɔman no mu
Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ banbɔ adwumayɛfoɔ no daeɛ bɛyɛ nnawɔtwe a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Burkina Faso so.
Na ɔne Bawku Naba wɔ akurase bi ase sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so wɔ Upper-East region no mu.
Ɔkwan a wɔfrɛ no Burkina Faso kɔɔ so no ma ayɛ hu sɛ mmoa a ɔredi saa nnipa bɔne yi ara na ɔnam kwan so agye yɛn nnwuma mu wɔ Ghana mantam mu.
Ɔkɔɔ so “Bawku Naba, wohunu sɛ aban retu anamɔn a ɔde strengthen asogyafoɔ a yɛfrɛ no ara bɔ yɛn ho ban afiri Burkina Faso hɔ.
“M’ani bɔ wo nkyerɛkyerɛ wo sɛ ahyɛ bɔne bi a ɛbɛkɔ so wɔ ɔman yi mu ha sɛ wɔbɛtumi ayɛ ankorɛankorɛ adwuma wɔ saa ara kwan yi so”
Mprenpren mu no, Bawku Naba a ɔsan yɛ Kusaug Kusaug Kusaug Kusaug Mantam mu, Asigiri Abugrago Azoka II kaa sɛ Ghanafoɔ nyansahufoɔ nyɛ adwuma ne Ghanafoɔ panin a ɔwɔ Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo dwumadie no ho mfasoɔ.
Wabɔ Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo wɔ ne electoral awiei no, "which ama Ghana yɛ wɔn nkwa wɔ mfeɛ ananmu a ɛtwa toɔ nu" kaa ho. Bawku Naba ka kyerɛɛ Ɔmanpanin no sɛ, "youi deɛ wabɔ mmɔden paa sɛ wobɛhwɛ saa dwumadie yi akyi. Mepɛ wo God'santo Ahoɔden Ahoɔden sɛ wobɛboa ma wo ayɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfata wɔ wo nhyehyɛeɛ no mu"
Child Rights International a woyɛɛ nsɔhwɛ mu kyerɛɛ sɛ nnipa mpem aduowɔtwe a ɛkɔdu baako ne aduonnwɔtwe a ɛyɛ 12 ne 17 a wɔsɔ ho no, ɛyɛ ɔha mu nkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛto Ghana ama greener pastures abroad.
Eleven percent kaa sɛ wɔn ho nteeɛ sɛ wɔbɛsɔ firi ɔman no mu anaa wɔn leaving ɔman no mu.
Wɔn a wɔyɛ ɔhaw mu nkyerɛ sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔkɔ ɔman foforɔ mu. Ɔka sɛ, wɔn mu ɔha mu nkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛte aba ɔman no mu na wɔn mu ɔha mu nkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛte aba ɔman no mu. Ɔka kyerɛɛ ɔhaw a wɔde wɔn ho anya nkɔsoɔ, adesua ne ahiadeɛ a ɛma wɔn nkɔsoɔ bɛma wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔbɛfiri ɔman yi mu.”
Sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ankonam wɔ ɔman yi mu a, wɔn a wobisaa toto dwumadie no ka sɛ: “Nea ɛka mu ɔha mu nkyerɛ sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ Ghana anya nsunsuansoɔ bɛyɛ mfeɛ aduonu (20). mfra biara mu ɔha mu nkyerɛ sɛ ɔman no anya nsunsuansoɔ bɛyɛ mfiri aduonu (20). Nnipa baanu biara mu nnipa ɔha mu nkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Mmabun bi a ɛwɔ Asante Mantam mu abɔ ahemfo bi kyerɛ sɛ wɔn nkyerɛkyerɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛwɔ Lighthouse Chapel International a ɛwɔ Amoaseɛ Mfinimfi Mantam mu Bere a asomdwoeɛ a ɔdaa nadi sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛ ahemfo bi a na ɔde reko atia Asante Monarch Otumfuo Osei Tutu.
Saa nsɛm yi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ abɛɛfo ntentan kɛseɛ no so no kyerɛ sɛ ɔde reka nsɛm a ɛho hia paa a influential king wɔ ne kyɛfa ne nkurɔfo ntentan no ho.
Sɛdeɛ ekuo no kyerɛ no, abranteɛ yi tenten a ɔyɛ televangelist yi ama odi kan no ɔhyɛ ɔpa kyɛn sɛ ɔde ne mfomso no bɛpa kyɛw.
“Yɛrehyɛ binom Pɔtɔnimaa bi so sɛ ɔbɛhwehwɛ wise counsel within 48 hours. Anyɛ saa a, n’akyerɛkyere bi nso wɔ Asanteman agyinamoa a ɛwɔ Asanteman manclave no so bɛsɔ ho. Also, yɛrehyɛ obiara a ɔde hia nyinaa ara sɛ ɔbɛbra Asanteman ne Otumfuo Osei Tutu haw ma wɔn. Yɛbɛma wɔn nkunim sɛ yɛbɛyɛ atuateɛ a ɛwɔ ɔhyehyɛ pa mu” Kwabena Frimpong kaa sɛ.
Bishop Dag Heward-Mills adi kan however ɔkaa sɛ ɔpa kyɛw wɔ sermon no mu.
Bere a ɔpa kyɛw no, Preacher kaa sɛ: “Mebɛyɛ da a mɛka asɛm bi ase wɔ conference a ɛtɔ so mmienu aduonu num (20 years ago) no akɔyɛ m’adwene na personfoɔ a ɔte saa di sɛ wɔn bɛfiri Kumase nhyiamu ase.
“Mepɛ sɛ mepa kyɛw wɔ His Majesty Otumfuo Nana Osei Tutu II sɛ ɔbɛrespect, insult anaa ɔyɛ biribi a ɛmfa ne koma wɔ ɔman no anim. Mesrɛ me kwan a statement yi ase”
National Democratic Congress amammuo panin, Kwasi Anim-Yeboah kyerɛɛ ne petition a ɔyɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin kyerɛɛ adwumakuo no, Dominic Ayine sɛ ɔnam kwan a ɔde ma ɔmfa nnipa ho dwiriw ano.
Dr Ayine wɔ nsɛm mu sɛ ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ Kɔɔto Baatan no mfa nhyɛɛ mmara so ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ asɛm yi mu. Ɔsan nso kyerɛ sɛ ɔkwan a ɛtoɔ no biara nnipa a wɔahwɛ petitioners’ applications during wahyɛ asɛm no mu.
Ɔkaa asɛm yi aberɛ a Ekuo a ɛhwɛ Centre for Democratic Development ne KNUST dii dwuma wɔ dwumadie mu.
Ɔtemmuafoɔ a Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin hyɛɛ GLC sɛ wɔmfa saa nsɛm yi ano na wɔnnye nnipa a wɔfa so yi asɛm.
Wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ase no, NDC panin paa, Johnson Asiedu Nketia frɛɛ onipa a ɔhwɛ ma Bolgatanga East MP no sɛ ɔmfa nnyɛ Petition no ntɛm ara.
“Ɔmanbuo a wɔwɔ sɛ atɛntenenee adwuma no gyina pintiin yɛn. Mpɛn pii ahe na woasɛe kɔɔto sɛ mɛma obi gyinaberɛ sɛ memfa asɛm no ho nanso mereka kɔkɔ sɛ wonka nsɛm? Owura Asiedu Nketia de too dwa sɛ General Mosquito kaa sɛ,
Ɔtoaa so sɛ, “Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu, te sɛ asɛmmuafoɔ anaa asɛmmuafoɔ no, nnyɛ criticism...Yɛ mmara ne constitution protect mmara a ɛho hia sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛ asɛmmuafoɔ a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔn din twerɛ wɔn din twerɛ wɔn din. Nsɛmmua a ɛwɔ sɛ ɔman no atɛnmua adwuma a ɛwɔ sɛ judicial arm of gov’t no nnyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛyɛ biara nti”
Owura Asiedu Nketia abɔ Kwantenpɔn Soafoɔ sɛ ɔnsosɔ NDC mmaranimfoɔ, na ɔreko atia mogya yi.
Ɔyɛɛ nwanwa sɛ ɔmaranimfoɔ a ɔda NDC adwumakuo no ano, Ɔtɛmmuafoɔ Panin, Justice Kwasi Anim Yeboah daa no adi sɛ ɔko a ɔda NDC adwumakuo no ano. Ɔyɛɛ asoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ sɛ ɔyɛ NDC mmaranimfoɔ a ɔde reyɛ adwuma na ɔnam so keka wɔn ho sɛ ɔne wɔn bɛyɛ nsɛm”
Akonta a ɛfiri Ghana abɛyɛ ɔman a ɛdi kan second wɔ Abibirem Africa behind Mauritius wɔ 2021 Peace Index a efi Akontabuo ne Asomdwoeɛ ho (IEP) kyerɛ no.
Global Peace Index yɛ wiase nyinaa a agye din wɔ wiase asomdwoeɛ mu. Wɔ index no mu ɛsono nnipa a ɛyɛ ɔman no agye wɔn ho sɛ wɔbɛyɛ asomdwoeɛ. Saa report yi kyerɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛfa nnipɔn a ɛbɛma asomdwoeɛ a ɛwɔ asomdwoeɛ mu na wɔbɛma asomdwoeɛ a ɛwɔ asomdwoeɛ mu.
Wɔ ɛka a wɔyɛɛ nhwehwɛmu no, so no mu no, Ghana bɔɔ ɔha aduonu num wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa ɛto so. Ghana boɔ yɛ ɔha aduoson baako, a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔde mmienu titiriw wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa.
Mauritius a ɛwɔ Abibirem ha na ɔman a asomdwoeɛ a ɛwɔ Abibirem no ayɛ ɔha aduonu num wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Ɔkɔɔ ɔha aduonu wɔ Abibirem no mu akyɛn wɔ Togo, Uganda, Kenya, The Republic of Congo ne Cameroon nso akyi.
Iceland remains ɔman a asomdwoeɛ a atwam sen biara wɔ wiase afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. yɛɛ nnwuma a New Zealand, Denmark, Portugal ne Slovenia wɔn ho ahyia.
Burkina Faso nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ wiase ɔha ne least a ɛtɔ so nan wɔ 2021 mu no akyi, followed by Yemen, Syria, South Sudan ne Iraq. Burkina Faso nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛtɔ so mmeɛnsa wɔ Global Peace Index afe 2021 mu no.
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no, nnipa a wɔwɔ Sub-Saharan Africa paa no, wɔn mu biara atu mpɔn. Wɔn a wɔtete Namibia no, wɔn nkurɔfo paa wɔ ɔha mu nkyɛmu dummiɛnsa ( 68%).
South Sudan nso wɔ ɔman a least asomdwoe mu wɔ region ne ɔman a least asomdwoe mu wɔ wiase afe yi mu, berɛ a asomdwoeɛ bosome wɔ afe 2021 awieɛ no mu.
Burkina Faso man a ɛtɔ so mmeɛnsa asomdwoeɛ wɔ any ɔman biara mu no kɔɔ so. Yei ne ɔman a ɛte paa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ aban yɛ nsiananfoɔ ahodoɔ a wɔde bɛhyehyɛ nnwuma mu no kɔɔ so. Aban no de ahyɛ nsiananfoɔ a wɔde bɛhyehyɛ nnwuma mu na ɛde hyɛ aseɛ no kɔ so.
Nsɛm no kyerɛɛ sɛ amanyɔsɛm mu ɔrewu ɛha mu nkyɛmu du kosi 10 per cent wɔ afe 2020 mu no. Nsɛm no kyerɛɛ sɛ: “Nka akyire ɛha mu nkyemu du kosi ɔha aduonu mpem ahanu na akuo ahodoɔ a ɛresɛe wɔn.”
Nsɛnkyerɛfoɔ kyerɛ sɛ, Covid yɛ deɛ “multiplying force” wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu ɛsiane amanyɔsɛm mu asotwe ne civil nko ara. Ɔkaa sɛ, sɛnea amanyɔsɛm mu rebɔ nkɔmmɔ a ɛbɛkɔ so no, gyina nea ɛbɛtumi ayɛ sikasɛm mu mpɛnpɛnso. Countries a ɛboa nnwuma ne asomdwoeɛ na wɔasan boa asomdwoeɛ mu na wɔbɛboa amanyɔsɛm mu ayɛ sikasɛm mpɛnpɛnso.
Nanso yei nti, nnipa mpem mmienu ne aduonnwɔtwe nyinaa mu no, wɔn mu baasa na wɔn ani gye ho sɛnea ɛtɔ so mmienu a atwam no afe mpem mmienu ne aduonnwɔtwe nnwɔtwe akyi no, na wɔwɔ nnipa a wɔwɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonnwɔtwe nnwɔtwe akyi no, afe mpem mmienu ne aduonnwɔtwe nnwɔtwe ahyɛ mu.
Afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako yi de, “ɛhaw a global asomdwoeɛ yɛ ɛfiri mu ɛyɛ ɔha-nkyɛmu dummienu wɔ 2021 Global Peace Index mu. wom sɛ asomdwoeɛ no rebɛyɛ ɛhaw mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu, na yei yɛ nea ɛtɔ so aduonu num wɔ mfeɛ mmienu ne aduonu num mu.
Nkabom apam no de kaa ho sɛ, “nnawɔtwe a atwa mu no, asomdwoeɛ mpem ɔha ne aduowɔtwe na ɛwɔ mu ayɛ nsakraeɛ. Nnipa mmeɛnsa a na wɔwɔ wɔn nkɔsoɔ no, wɔwɔ wiase aduasa nso na wɔn nkɔsoɔ no mu ayɛ nsakraeɛ. Wɔn a wɔwɔ wiase asomdwoeɛ no mu ayɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ wiase afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe mu. Nnipa mmeɛnsa a wɔwɔ wiase no mu ayɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ wiase afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe mu. However,
Europe.nea ɛbɛyɛ asomdwoeɛ a wɔwɔ wiase so wɔ wiase no mu. Ɔman no mu fa a ɛdi mu ɔha ne aduowɔtwe a wɔwɔ Europa ho no, na biom nso ɔman biara wɔ Europe ho no yɛ pɛpɛɛpɛɛpɛ.
Ɔmanpanin a ɔhyɛɛ ɔmanpanin-elect Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo-Addo ama Ghanafoɔ awerɛhyɛmu sɛ wɔn bɛnya nneɛma ani wɔ ne presidency no mu.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ nna kakra a afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe no bɛtumi ama Ghanani abɛyɛ adwuma.
“Meho hia paa sɛ mfeɛ bɛyɛ aduasa nnwɔtwe a ɛtwa toɔ mu no bɛnya nnipa a ɛwɔ Ghana amanfoɔ aba so” Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire daa na ɔkɔɔ Nigeria berɛ a wahyɛ presidential abatoɔ no mu.
Owura Akufo-Addo rekasa wɔ ɔmanpanin a ɔwɔ Nigeria Owelle Rochas Anayo Okorocha a ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ: “ Ghana sikasɛm ne nnwuma akɔ so wɔ mfeɛ mmienu ato mu nanso yɛn adwene yɛ nneɛma a ɛwɔ sɛ yɛde bɛma ɔman no ayɛ anikasɛm afiri hɔ nanso yɛwɔ nneɛma a ɛwɔ sɛ yɛde bɛma ɔman no ayɛ anikasɛm afiri hɔ.”
Ɔmanpanin a ɔyi abasobɔ wɔ amanyɔkuo Ɔmanpanin John Dramani Mahama wɔ abatoɔ a ɛtɔ so mmienu yi mu no wɔ ɔkɔɔ Nigeria awiei ne oil producing country Ɔmanpanin, Muhammudu Buhari.
Owura Akufo-Addo hyɛɛ Imo mpaninfoɔ bɔ sɛ ɔman no faako a ɛwɔ Abibirem Africa Aman no bɛdi dwuma wɔ ne presidency no mu.
“Yɛwɔ ho sɛ asomdwoeɛ a ɛkɔ so wɔ saa man yi mu. yɛ ho sɛ yɛbɛmia yɛn manfoɔ ne yɛn kankɔ wɔ asafo no mu. ma yɛn manfoɔ anya nwerɛhyɛmu sɛ yɛrebɛsi wɔn ɔhaw ahodoɔ na yɛma wɔn mpuntuo nso anya nkɔsoɔ wɔ wɔn daakye”
Ɔmanpanin John Dramani Mahama ahyɛ Joseph Whittal sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ama Commission on Human Rights ne Administrative Justice (CHRAJ) no.
Na Owura Whittal asɛm hyɛɛ aseɛ wɔ dwumadie bi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Flagstaff House da a ɛtɔ so nnɔ no.
Owura Whittal abɛdiakyire sɛ ɔpanin abadiakyire, Lauretta Vivian Lamptey no wɔ CHRAJ berɛ a Ɔmanpanin abadiakyire abadiaa no too hɔ berɛ a na ɔrehwehwɛ ɔman no nkorabata.
Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire, Ms. Josephine Nkrumah asɛ ɔbaa National Commission for Civic Education (NCCE) no.
Owura Nkrumah a ɔdii kan pɛ sɛ wɔn nhyiamu a amanyɔkuo no kura no. Owura Charlotte Osei a ɔdii kan pɛ sɛ ɔmanpanin abadiakyire wɔ Ɔgyefuo da a ɛtɔ so afe baako mu.
Saa nhyiamu yi baa mmerɛ kakra a Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo de too dwa no.
Ɔmanpanin a wabɔ ne sɛ wɔhyɛɛ ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire no January 7, 2017.
GN Apɔmuden Adwumakuo, one of the 75 companies of Groupe Nduom fa Ambulance Services a ɛwɔ Ghana.
Ƹbɛhyɛ bɔ sɛ wɔde reyɛ apɔmuden asoeɛ a ɛbɛba fam ama wɔn ahwehwɛ ɔhaw a emu yɛ den.
GN Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ dwumadie no bɛboa ama ayarehwɛ ɔhaw ne nsunsuansoɔ a yɛfrɛ no intervention.
Ɔpanin a ɔda GN Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ Issah Adam ne “once again the Ɔpanin a ɔda Groupe Nduom, Dr Papa Kwesi Nduom ne ne baasonfoɔ panin, Owura Yvonne Nduom ne mpaninfoɔ rehyɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ aseɛ wɔ berɛ a ɔde reboa adwumayɛfoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no”
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Yei kyerɛɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ a ɔte saa yi mu ma yenya mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmmubea a ɛdi kan a yɛfrɛ no Nduom Medical Services mu. Nea ɛwɔ sɛ wɔde bɛpagya apɔmuden adwumayɛ mu na wɔde Ambulance Service de complete the apɔmuden mu ama adwumayɛfoɔ a ɛwɔ Nkran ne Mfinimfi Mantam mu nyinaa.”
Sɛdeɛ available statistics kyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ no, ahwehwɛ ambulance no sɛ wɔde akɔgya ɛmmaa labour ne accident victim ho kɔɔ ayaresabea apɛn apɔmuden. Animdefoɔ gye di sɛ ɛwɔ hɔ a ahwehwɛ mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ahwehwɛ no ama wɔayɛ apɔmuden te sɛ nea GN Apɔmuden Adulance Adwuma no pɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ.
“GN Apɔmuden bɛma yɛnya EMTs (Emergency Medical Technicians) ne Ambulance Ɔdɔmfoɔ a wɔntetee wɔn paa, na wɔnim nea yɛyɛ wɔ ɔhaw mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ “The Ford 350 ambulance no ɛpagya nneɛma a wahyehyɛ mfidie ne aduan a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔde wɔn ahyɛ anamɔn a ɛwɔ ayaresabea. Please take note sɛ ambulance no ɛnnyɛ transport dwumadie a ɛbɛma wɔayɛ apɔmuden a ɛmfa agye ntentanhunu”
Ambulances no wɔ ahorow a wɔde reyɛ mfidie biara a wɔde hwehwɛ adɔyankorabea. Wɔn a wɔwɔ ahorow yɛ mfidie biara a wɔde yɛ hwehwɛ adɔyankorabea no mu, fidie a wɔde yɛ defibrillators ne defibrillators. Yɛn adwuma yɛ nneɛma bi te sɛ bandages ne disinfectant solution.

Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ ɔtanhunu ano, Dr Matthew Opoku Prempeh aka sɛ aban de reboa Ghana mpuntuo a ɛnam abɛɛfo nnwuma ne renewables mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ mu no nnipa bi sɛ wɔbɛtumi akɔ so sɛ nuclear energy yɛ decarbonising mfidie nkabom reba mfidie ahodoɔ a wɔbɛtumi de aba asɛm no mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Wɔ agyinaeɛ foforɔ renewable energy so a, wɔbɛtumi akɔ so yie paa. Nnwuma a ɛka ho asɛm wɔ nnwuma mu no yɛ nnyinasoɔ a ɛbɛboa ama advanced economie agye baabiara, na wɔde bɛboaa nnipa 40 percent wɔ ama agyinaeɛ a wɔde renewable energy generation mu.
Ɔredi International Energy Agency dwumadie a ɔde ma ɔkwan a yɛrebue mframa yi ho asserɛ sɛ, sɛ ɛnyɛ kilomita baako pɔtee a yɛrebue mframa yi ho a, ɛbɛyɛ den ama emissions, cost ne energy security.
Dr Opoku Prempeh kaa asɛm yi, wɔ nsɛm a wɔne nea wɔresɛe no Stakeholders Forum a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Ghana Nuclear Power Programme a ɛwɔ Nkran no.
Ɔfiri tema: “Nuclear Energy Innovations: The Future Technologies for Clean Energy ne ɛkwan a wɔfa so de ahyɛ nsaaseɛ apɔmuden dwumadie a ɛhyɛ aseɛ wɔ Ghana Nsuo Adwumakuo no (AGI) ne Nclear Power Ghana (NPG) na wɔhyehyɛ aseɛ.
Dr Opoku Prempeh asua sɛ wɔrehye mfidie ahodoɔ a wɔde sika hye no mu nso decarbonise mmeɛnsa wɔ mmeɛnsa ho ne nneɛma foforo a wɔde bɛhye nsuo ho dwuma.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Adeɛ ɛma Ghana akwan foforɔ a yɛrebue no, ɛhaw a yɛnya ɛboɔ no, akwan a yɛnya so deɛ ɛboɔ yɛ adwuma, affordability, reliability ne resilience criteria a ɛkɔ ma ayɛ ɔhaw foforɔ a yɛrebue no”
Ɔkaa sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ aban yɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no nyinaa akyi no, ahwɛ ne nneɛma foforo a ɛba saa, nso wɔbɛtumi atwe nea ɛbɛtumi ayɛ ama ɔman no nyinaa tetewa.
“Aseɛ foforɔ a ɛbɛyɛ ato hɔ ma anyinam ahoɔden wɔ mu a, ɛma ɛnya mfasoɔ biara mfasoɔ wɔ dwumadie a ɛdi kan no ho bɛyɛ nnipa mfeɛ aduonu 60 bɛyɛ adwuma.”
Ɔkaa sɛ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu no, Ɔmanpanin John Agyekum Kufuor de ahyɛ asoafoɔ a wɔfrɛ no Daniel Adzei-Bekoe de rehwehwɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛtumi de Ghana using nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-nu-no mu de rehyɛ aseɛ.
Na eyi anɔpa a Ghana ɔhyɛɛ supply power ahorow dwumadie mu.
Ɔsan de aba mpuntuo akwankyerɛfoɔ rema ɔman no abɛɛfo kwan so mpuntuo nnyinasoɔ ho no, ɔkaa sɛ aban ahyɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi ama ɔman no nnyinasoɔ ahodoɔ no bɛba ɔkwankyerɛ ne akadeɛ a ɛbɛboa ama ɔman no nnuanom nsawɔsoɔ.
Yei ama NPG abɛyɛ adwumakuo no sɛ ɛyɛ Ghana kanea a ɛtɔ so mmienu.
Ɔkaaɛ sɛ NPG Board no ne Owura Fred Oware na ɔhyɛeɛ sɛ wɔnnyae akwankyerɛ a wɔde bɛboa asraafoɔ ma wɔbɛnya apɔmuden ne nhyehyɛeɛ akwankyerɛ a wɔfa so di dwuma wɔ nsakraeɛ a wɔyɛɛ apɔmuden ne nhyehyɛeɛ dwuma wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Nneɛma a ɛwɔ ato hɔ sɛ wɔde rema anyinam ahoɔdennuru a ɛba saa dwumadie yi mu no betumi ama wɔayɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ asaase foforɔ mu a ɛbɛma wɔanya mfidie ahoɔdennuru a wɔde yɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ nnwuma mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, "Wɔde abɛɛfo mfiri kɔmputa so reboa nkurɔfo asetena wɔ mpuntuo nnwuma mu, na wɔaboa ama mpontuo aba mpuntuo nso"

Tax stamps a ɛda toɔ wɔ alcoholic ne non-alcoholic beverages ho akɔ mfeɛ mmienu no apagya sika ho mfasoɔ.
Afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe a ɛyɛ sika ɔpepem aduonu nan ase afe 2018 mu no, asɛe sika no kɔpepem baako aduasa mmienu ne aduowɔtwe a ɛyɛ ɔha-nkyɛmu nan aduonu mmienu wɔ afe 2020 mu, na mpaninfoɔ de project no reyɛ adwuma sɛ ɔpepem aduasa ɔha-nkyɛmu nan aduasa mmienu ne aduonu baako wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
Ghana Revenue Authority (GRA) se ɔsan nso yɛ adwumakuo a ɛwɔ Ghana (FABAG) ne adwadifoɔ nnwumakuo a ɛwɔ wɔn nnuanom (FABAG) ne wɔn a wɔde wɔn nnuanom (FABAG) ne wɔn a wɔde wɔn nnuanom te sɛ wɔtwe wɔn beverage dwumadie no mu.
Ghanani printing company, Buck Press ne ne sam, DelaRue a ɔyɛ British security printing company, reyɛ adwuma de wɔn nsa frɛ GRA na Streamline Resources a ɛwɔ Tema Port no, assistsɛ adwumakuo a wɔwɔ nneɛma ho kwan sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nneɛma a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔde stamps no ho adi dwuma.
Project Manager of Excise Tax Stamp a GRA dwumadie, Owura Kwabena Apau Awuah Anto a ɔde kaa ho sɛ, saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi bɛboa ama adwadifoɔ ne nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ a wɔredi product fraud ne piracy, where importers ne manufacturers de nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ yi de too dwa sɛ wɔmfa nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ a ɛfiri FDA hɔ, nanso wɔde afa ahodoɔ bi a wɔhyɛ no safety certification from the Food and Drugs Authority (FDA) hɔ.
Ɔrekasa wɔ nsrahwɛ toɔ a yɛfrɛ no din wɔ Tema Port dwumadie a ɛyɛ Graphic Communications Group Limited (GCGL) reka no, Owura Anto daa no adi sɛ GRA asoeɛ no ahyɛ mmaa nnipa 34 a wɔimporters ne manufacturers, including Guinness Ghana Limited ne Coca-Cola Bottling Company, sɛ wɔde twaa toɔ no ho mfasoɔ wɔ wɔn factories mu.
Ɔtemmuafoɔ a ɔda GGCL adwuma no ano ne Managing Director, Owura Ato Afful ne Daily Graphic, Owura Kobby Asmah; the Director, Marketing, Mr Franklin Sowa ne the Editor of The Mirror, Ms Doreen Hammond.
Na yɛn asuafoɔ no wɔ Tema na wɔbɛkaa sɛ wɔn anya nkitahodie afa mfeɛ aduonu baako mu na GRA nso oyikyerɛ wɔn nko ara sɛ wɔbɛfa saa dwumadie yi akyi.
Owura Anto kaa sɛ excise stamp policy no bɛbue nnwuma kwan na ɛbɛbue Kwan sɛ ɛbɛyɛ nnwuma a ɛbɛboa ama manfoɔ ayɛ mmerɛw ne banbɔ.
Ɔkaa sɛ, nhyehyɛeɛ ahodoɔ no bɛboa sikasɛm mu assurance, na ɛbɛboa ama adwadifoɔ ne nnipa nnwuma akɔ so sɛ wɔbɛtumi ayɛ wɔn ho to ntomu a ɛfata wɔ toɔ mu.
Owura Anto kaa sɛ: “Yɛde yɛn yɛn mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmmubea a ɛwɔ Tema dan ne 13 a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu a wɔwɔ affixing dwuma no ɛnyɛ boɔ ma abotɔyamfoɔ.
Ɔkaaɛ sɛ dan no ho akadeɛ no yɛ nneɛma a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔde ka stamps, utility, labour, operational cost ne nneɛma a wɔde shrink wrap no ho.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Berɛ a nhyehyɛeɛ yi kɔɔ so afe 2018 mu no, aban no sii gyinaeɛ sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn ntaadeɛ no boɔ yie nanso ɛnam so kɔɔ so ɛda no adi sɛ wɔnnye nnipa a wɔde sika no bɛtua wɔn no, hence asɛm Asoeɛ no nsɛm a ɛfa wɔn ntua ɛho hia sɛ wɔbɛtua wɔn no.
Nkitahodie no, Owura Anto kaa sɛ, dwumadie no bɛkɔ so ahwehwɛ sɛ GRA no bɛhyɛ no boɔ ase ɛna ɛbɛsisi nkurɔfoɔ a wɔwɔ kyɛfa wɔ nnwuma no mu.
Wɔ aman bi a ɛwɔ Kenya no, akwammafoɔ bepia sɛ wɔde saa nnipa yi ma wɔn. Enti sɛ wɔkɔ so a, wɔma wɔn nneɛma a wɔde di dwuma yɛ adwuma.
Ghana nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛda toɔ stamp dwumadie no de ɛda toɔ a affected excise product no so nti, ɛyɛ ɔmfa toɔ no baako anaa ɔmfa toɔ no manufacturer.
Wɔ mmeaɛ bi a saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi bɛma wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma no, mfidie ahodoɔ biara wɔ wɔn production unit no mu” Owura Anto kaa sɛ.
Ɔkwan a ɛte saa haw a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛtemmuafoɔ nnwuma a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ teɛbea no mu no, Owura Anto kyerɛɛ mu sɛ Tema facilities no ɛnhia sɛ nnipa a ɛkɔɔ so wɔn nnwuma mu no na mmom nnipa a wɔimportu dwumadie mma no nnya ɔhaw bi.
Nanso, ɔkaa sɛ, nnipa a wɔde sika kɔkɔɔ dwadie no bɛtɔɔ dwa a affixing no ma wɔde wɔn nnwuma no ho nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛda hɔ sɛ wɔmfa nneɛma nkɔsoɔ too nko ara na ɛde akwannya bebree akwankyerɛfoɔ no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a akwannya bebree bɛgu so.
Saa ara nso na ɛyɛ ɔhaw a ɛde reba abɛɛfo asoeɛ no nso resulti wɔn ntɛm ara, ɔedwene ho.
Nanso mfididwumayɛfoɔ yɛ wɔn mmoa ma wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ ase.
Ɔrekasa no, Owura Asmah frɛɛ GRA ma wɔn nsakraeɛ wɔ adwuma a ɛrekɔ so wɔn trade space mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔde toto ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ toa mu no ho firisɛ ɛbɛboa ama wɔn anya nkitahodie na aboa ama wɔn short-change the system no.
Ɔhyɛɛ GRA mpaninfoɔ, Streamline Resources, ne adwumakuo a wɔhwɛ GRA soboɔ aba so sɛ wabɔ ɔhaw ahodoɔ yi.
Ɔkaa sɛ, GRA ne ɛmu yɛɛn ntamgyinafoɔ no bɛfa ato hɔ ma excise tax stamp dwumadie yi akɔ so nkyerɛ sɛ ɔnyaa nteaseɛ wɔ dwumadie yi mu.
“Megye di sɛ yei yɛ akwannya berɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman ne GRA anim sɛ wɔn bɛko ama ɔmanfoɔ anim.” Owura Asmah kaa sɛ.
Ekuo a ɛhwɛ ɛma Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ (IES) se, sika a wɔde ma fango ho nneɛma boɔ yɛ deɛ ɛboɔ ma pumps. Ɔkaaeɛ a IES kyerɛɛ sɛ, sika a wɔde fuel ho nneɛma wɔ local market no increased within the window under review mu.
Ayɛwohomumɔ bosome a ɛdi kan wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu no, fango adwumakuo no (OMCs) nyaa boɔ wɔn prices of petroleum products mu gyina ɔha mu nkyemu dummiɛnsa mu. Based on this increase no, ɛreyɛ a ɔman no boɔ nyinaa ara wɔ GHS5.97, na ɛbɛgyina gasoline ne fango mu.
Yɛde akwantuo ɛberɛ yi, Zen Petroleum, Benab Oil, Cash Oil, Goodness Oil, Top Oil ne Frimps Oil no de ba baabi a yɛde ma ɛnyɛ adwuma wɔ local market no mu, sɛdeɛ IES market scan no mu.
Ɔkwan a wɔyɛ nneɛma yi mu no, international benchmark Brent crude boɔ no boɔ yɛ $73.98 per barrel, a ɛgyina ɔpepem baako ne mmiɛnsa mu ɔha mu nkyɛmu dɔla a na wɔyɛɛ ɔpepem aduasa nnwɔtwe.
Adeɛ a etwaam no ɛpagya wɔ atɔeɛ aseɛ berɛ a na ɛresɛe COVID-19 yadeɛ a ɛda Delta variant a ɛwɔ Europa ne amumuyɛ a ɛda hɔ wɔ United States.
Fiti mmerɛ mfeɛ mmienu no, boɔ bi a wɔde sika bɛto Brent no atɔ ne boɔ yɛ Amerika sika no 75. nnɛ crude boɔ no yɛ adwuma sɛ awahyehyɛ aseɛ aberɛ a wɔatoto nneɛma mu awieɛ na amamfra ahodoɔ rehyɛ aseɛ.
Yei ne titire deɛ, berɛ a akwan ne kwantenpɔn adwuma no akɔ soro.
Brent crude boɔ ahyɛ aseɛ nso yɛ nneɛma a ɛresɛe nneɛma foforɔ a ɛwɔ Europe, Asia ne Mfinimfi Mantam mu, berɛ a yɛnyaa ɛne nneɛma mpɛsɛmpɛsɛmu a ɛwɔ wɔ period mu no.
July a ɛtɔ so bosome wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe nyinaa ho no, wɔbɛhyehyɛ aseɛ na ɛsɔ berɛ a yɛbɛkɔ Ɔsram bosome no.
Nteeɛ ne sɛ, Fango ne Fango atɔeɛ a wɔhwɛ Standard ne Poor’s global Platts dwumadie no kyerɛ sɛ, aman ahoɔden a wiase wɔ wiase no, no ɛgyinaeɛ a ɛboɔ bɛsesa nneɛma pii (petrol) ne ɛgasoil (diesel) no kɔɔ soro.
Gasoline deɛ, ɛkyɛn boɔ mu ɔha mu ɔpepem baako dɔla akyire pɔtee no, na bɛyɛɛ no ɔpepem aduonu mmienu($694.78), sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔfrɛ no ɔpepem aduonu mmienu no, na wɔsan de boɔ yɛ no ɔpepem aduonu mmienu($671.45).
Gasoil nnwuma no kɔɔ so mpɛnpɛnsoɔ tuu mpɛnsoɔ ahanu adwuma no mu ɔha-nkyɛmu aduonum, na wɔatoto boɔ yɛ ɔpepem mmienu aduonu($597.30), sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔatoto boɔ no mu yɛ ɔpepem mmienu aduonu($569.88), na wɔatoto boɔ no mu ɛnyɛ ɔpepem mmienu aduonu($569.88).
Data a IES’ Economic Desk kyerɛɛ wɔ Foreign Exchange (Forex) market no mu kyerɛ sɛ cedi no yɛ ketewaa mu ɔpepem aduonu nan so, daa no adi sɛ ɛdi bɛyɛ GH5.77 kɔɔ US dollar.

Aban no hyɛɛ agitafoɔ no sɛ wɔn calm wɔn ase.

Nanso nokwarem no, ɔhaw a ɛwɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwani no mu a na ɔresɛe regime no sɛ wɔmfata atikyafoɔ no ara na ɔreka wɔn ho sɛ wɔn mmoa wɔn ho.
Afei, yɛn Polisi nkorabata a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔbɛtete saa agitatorsfoɔ yi ɛmmɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛmfa Covid asɛm no ho mfasoɔ. Enti sɛ wɔn twaa saa agitatorsfoɔ yi ɛna wɔn ani na wɔn awerɛhyɛ nnipa a ɛwɔ Sir John funeral no ho mfasoɔ.
ka sɛ ɔman no yɛ nneɛma bi pɔtee a ɔde amanyɔsɛm ho anamɔn a ɔde ɔne atikyafoɔ agye n’anim no, ɛyɛ den ni na sɛ ɔkyerɛw ebinom sɛ ɔne asɛm no nyinaa mfasoɔ bɛtwe ebinom sɛ ɔne n’anim no nyɛɛ huhuhuhu.
sɛ sɛ yɛn nim sɛ, ɛnsɛ sɛ yɛn bo ase na yɛbɛhwɛ amanyɔsɛm mu mpo a, ɛbɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔnsosɔne aban no bɔne akɔ soro, esiane sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ na aban no ayɛ baabiara amanyɔsɛm.
Nnyinasoɔ biara nni hɔ a ebetumi aboa Kaaka no awu.

Sɛ ignorantnifoɔ a wɔwɔ asraafoɔ nko ara na ɔkɔɔ killɔ nnipa mmienu a wɔwɔ mu no, mɛtwe wɔn ho kɔkɔ.

Aban bɛpɛ sɛ wɔbɛfiri banbɔfoɔ a wɔnnyae din sɛ ɛbɛma wɔn a wɔyɛ asogyafoɔ no dae adi dwuma a ɛbɛma yɛn asogyafoɔ daakye kɔkyere wɔ asafo no ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛyɛ a wɔmmɔ wɔn asogyafoɔ daakye. Aban nso pɛ sɛ wɔbɛsan akɔkyere wɔn asogyafoɔ a wɔwɔ mmɔdenmmɔ ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛtumi akɔ kɔɔto akɔkyere ɛho nhia, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛ
Eyi nkogu nkyerɛ sɛ ɛma ɔdɔ ntɛm saa na ɛma ɔdɔ no nkyɛn agu.
Ɔmanpanin ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ assurancefoɔ ma ɔbɛma asomdwoeɛ a ɛwɔ asaseɛ mu aba asɛm yi nyinaa ara.
Asraafoɔ a wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu no nni nsɛm wɔ agitators ne adeɛ yi so.
Ƹhaw a yɛn Peace Council dwumadie no abɔ mu ama ekuo no legitimacy deficit a ɛbɛma Ekuo no ayɛ nnipa a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔn ankasa yɛ adwuma. Ɔsom ahodoɔ yi ara nti, Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire bɛtumi ayɛ n’ahodoɔ na ɛwɔ sɛ ɔyɛ nneɛma mmoa.
Thomas Amoani a wadi mfeɛ aduonu nsia wɔ Adeiso Presbyterian Senior High School a ɔwɔ Ghana Scholarships Secretariat so no akyerɛ sɛ ɔboaa Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo Addo.
Thomas Amoani, a who had eight A‘s wɔ West Africa Secondary School Certificate Examination no mu daa no adi sɛ wɔbɛgye scholarship na wɔresua adesua wɔ Brunel University a ɛwɔ London berɛ a na ɔde krataa futofoɔ a yɛfrɛ no Kingsley Agyemang.
Owura abarimaa bi a ne mfe 19 a wɔfrɛ no Adeiso ne abusuakuw a ne nnyinasoɔ yɛ Asuaba, a ɛwɔ Adeiso na ne nnyinasoɔ yɛ Adwuma ne Sikasɛm ne Sikasɛm ne Sikasɛm ne Sikasɛm ne nnwuma.
Nsɛm a ɔka Adeiso SHS dwumadie no daa adi pefee berɛ a na ɔne abɛɛfo kwantempɔn mu Thomas Amoani recounterɛ ɔkwan a na ɔde rekɔ fam akwan 12 kilomita baako mu.
Na asɛm yi maa Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo a ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔnnyaa dwumadie a ɔde scholarship no mu.
Wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ krataa a ɔde maa no nsɛntwerɛfoɔ bebree wɔ Scholarship Secretariat no mu no, Registrar kaa sɛ honour done Thomas a ɔmanpanin no bɛsi nkaneɛ bɛsi afoforo ama wɔn mpɛsɛmpɛsɛ mu.
“Me de Thomases foforɔ ahyɛ wɔn ase na mereka bɔ sɛ Scholarships Secretariat bɛhwɛ wɔn ma wɔn anya mmoa pa ara sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn mpae. Thomas nneyɛɛ bɔne sɛ ɛbɛma others like him. Ɔsɛ sɛ memaa Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo adi dwuma so wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ a ɔde n’anim yi baaeɛ.” Owura Agyemang kaa sɛ.
Thomas Amoani a ɔrewura sukuu no haw no ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔde rema Ghana kankɔ ɛna ɔmfa Ghana ho nkɔmɔ na ɔmma ɔman no down.
“Mansusuw da sɛ me bɛnya saa kwan ama Owura manpanin firisɛ wɔn adwumayɛfoɔ ne wɔn nteteɛ Registrar so. Merekasa yi ma me yagye amanbuo a ɛboa ma me. Menka ɔman no Ghana bɔɔ.”
Brunel University London yɛ ɔman mu nhwehwɛmu a wɔyɛ nsawɔsoɔ wɔ Uxbridge area of London, England. Founded in 1966 and named after the Victorian engineer Isambard Kingdom Brunel, ɛyɛ apɔmuden a wɔwɔ suban nnwuma wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa, na wɔhwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ apɔmuden a wɔwɔ wiase afanan nyinaa, a na wɔhwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nsawɔsoɔ wɔ mu.
nyɛ ɔhaw kwan sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin, Justice Kwasi Anim Yeboah fi agyinaeɛ kɔkɔ atia ɔhwɛ sɛ ɔyɛ mmaranimfoɔ, Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine fi Aban Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu wɔ General Legal Council (GLC) no.
Sɛdeɛ ɔman mmarahyɛbɛdwani ne Owura John Ndebugre kyerɛɛ mu sɛ, National Democratic Congress (NDC) ne nkurɔfoɔ a wɔsusu sɔhwɛ no yɛ nsɛm nti na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ de Dr Ayine appears before the Disciplinary Committee of the General Legal Council (GLC) no.
“Menim sɛ ɔne (Dr. Ayine) na ɔwɔ animtiaa sɛ ɔnni asɛm yi mu firisɛ Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Panin a ɔde abɛdiakyire yi anim no ne sɛ, yɛkyerɛ mu sɛ n’asoeɛ a ɛwɔ sɛhwɛ ama mmara ho adwuma no twe wɔ ɔkwan bi so a”
Chief Justice asrɛɛ abɔdiakyire Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine kɔɔto GLC mpaninfoɔ sɛ nsɛm a ɔkaa wɔ abatoɔ asoeɛ nhyiamu a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Abibirem Mantam mu no nnyinasoɔ a ɛwɔ Afrika Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu.
Dr. Ayine abɔ asɛnnibea kɔɔ sɛ ɔmmra Judiciary nwɔtwe wɔ 2020 abatoɔ anodisɛm mu berɛ a ɔman no Kɔɔto Baatan no atɛmmuo nnyinaa.
Petition no se Dr. Ayine a ɔkaeɛ sɛ nsɛm a ɔde baa asɛm yi mu berɛ akasakasa no ne Kɔɔto Baatan no nnyinasoɔ a ɛbɛma Kɔɔto Baatan no ahofama ne ɔtweeɛ a ɛrekɔ so yi.
“Saa nsɛm yi reba ɔman yi hyɛɛ aseɛ maa ɔtemmuafoɔ a ɔda Kɔɔto Baatan no ano, Dr. Ayine hyɛɛ mfomsoɔ sɛ ɔkasaa mfeɛ aduonu nsia a ɔyii nnipa a ɔwɔ Kɔɔto anim berɛ a saa nsɛm yi reba ɔman no anim.”
Dr. Ayine, ne ɔkyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛtɔ so mmeɛnsa yi wɔ CJ abatoɔ no so ase no, nnyɛ sɛ ɔkaa sɛ ɔde nisuo atɛntenenee a atɛnmuafoɔ a wɔtɔw ama abatoɔ no ano.
Ɔkyerɛ sɛ n’asɛm no reka nokware.
“Asɛdeɛ yi asɛm a mekyerɛw wɔ saa asɛm yi ho no, sɛ meyɛ mmaranimfoɔ a, mɛyɛ ɔkandifoɔ ma ɔde m’adwuma atu asɛm no mu. By nteteeɛ ne experience mu, m’ani gye ho bɛn na ɛbɛyɛ me fellow manfoɔfoɔ a wɔmfa asɛm yi ho adwene nhyɛ so”
Ɔkɔɔ so kaa sɛ n’asɛm no ɛsɛ sɛ nea ɔkaeɛ no temperate speech mu.
Amanyɔkuo a ɛwɔ Nkran, National Democratic Congress (NDC) wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ase wɔ Nkran no, Wukuada, Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Nkran, Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ nsɛm yi mu sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin no gye saa akyi no, Owura Ndebugre kaa sɛ, Dr. Ayine nso na ɔrekasa anaa panel no nnipa a ɔnya ɔhaw no ho dwuma, na ɔrekasa nso na ɔreka saa akyi no. Ɔkaa sɛ ɔde rehwɛ mmara ho kwan sɛnea Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin no nnyɛ ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin, na ɔno nso na ɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu.
Berɛ a Owura Ndebugre rekasa wɔ NTV rekasa wɔ Nkran Kwasiada anɔpa a ɛtɔ so aduonu nson wɔ 2021 mu no, Owura Ndebugre kaa sɛ: "Mepɛ sɛ ɔhaw nnipa dodoɔ a Ɔtemmuafoɔ no de akwankyerɛ no so"
Comparing that to what happened afe 1996 - the Republic against Mensah Bonsu, Stephen Quarcoo ne Tommy Thompson - ɛno mu no Mensah Bonsu attackɔ ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ, Justice Abban ɛnti ɔde too dwa gyinaeɛ a ɔtoo dwa no mu, ɛno na ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ wɔmfa asɛm no nyinaa firisɛ Attorney-General kɔɔ firi hɔ kɔɔ firisɛ ɔmfa asɛm no nyinaa too mu anaa Attorney-General kɔɔ firii hɔ kɔɔ firisɛ ɔmfa asɛm no nyinaa too mu.
Ɔpɛ sɛ CJ filing complaint ano?
“Enti m’adwene sɛ ɔhaw Ɔtemmuafoɔ a Ɔde asomdwoeɛ no bɛnya no so.
Asɛm a ɛwɔ ho ne sɛ, Dominic Ayine yɛ Ɔsoafoɔ Panin, na ɔne ne baasonfo yi tuo wɔn kɔɔ criminal court no, proceeding kɔɔ civil court no... Ɔso sɛ Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ panyin abɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔmmra obi a wadi mfɛnsoɔ wɔn kɔkyerɛ sɛ no, ɔmfa Kwaadubɔfoɔ wadi mfɛnsoɔ wɔn kɔɔto.
No, ɛsɛ sɛ wobɛkɔ akɔgyinatɔ kɔɔto na wɔkyerɛ w’asɛm no mu, na wɔkyerɛ sɛ wonni bɔne no nto wo deɛ.
Enti Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin no nyinasoɔ gye sɛ asɛm no ɛsɛ sɛ asɛm no bu mmara ho kwan sɛ ɔbɛyɛ asɛm adwuma no.
“ Yei go there, all those akwansideɛ a NDC ne Dr Ayine himself reka no ɛyɛ nneɛma a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde bɛba Badwam no Disciplinary Committee no nyinaa bɛba abɔ mu.” Owura Ndebugre seeɛ.
Berɛ a ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ n’adwene nhyiam no ho nhwɛso no, ɔdaa no adi sɛ, sɛ wobɛka sɛ ɔsom bo afuw a, ɛyɛ te sɛ ne ho ase, na berɛ a asɛm no puee afaafa no, ɛno ne sɛ wobɛfa asɛm no ho anim na w’adwene nhyia wɔ asɛm no mu, ɛno ne sɛ wobɛfa asɛm no ho anim na w’adwene nhyia wɔ asɛm no mu, wobɛkɔ atia ɛno ho.
Sɛ wunya asɛm no kɔɔ kɔɔto a, wubetumi aka sɛ wunnim ɔkwan biara so, "nanso sɛ meka sɛ mɛpɛ sɛ memmfa asɛm no ho nti, nea meyɛ saa ara ne sɛ memfa asɛm no ho nti, ɛfirisɛ ɛyɛ me sɛ wobɛgye asɛm no ho nti, ɛyɛ me nso sɛ wobɛgye asɛm no nti, na ɛfirisɛ ɛyɛ me sɛ wobɛgye asɛm no nti, Ɔyɛ me nnyɛ adwene."
“No point no ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wobɛkɔ Kɔɔto Baanodani Asoeɛ no Disciplinary Committee na wokyerɛkyerɛ mu sɛ woreyɛ wɔn nkyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛwɔ nsɛm ho ano, nanso ɛnte sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin nka ho sɛ wamu wɔn sɛ ɔkyerɛ asɛm no ho mmuaeɛ, ɛno na wobɛka sɛ wɔn anya nnyinasoɔ wɔ Kɔɔto Baanodani no ho nti. Ɔwɔ sɛ ɔkɔɔ hɔ [GLC] na ɔkyerɛkyerɛ nsɛm a ɛde nhyɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ no a ɛde
Ɔkɔɔ so rekasa afa nsɛm yi sɛ Ɔtɛmmuafoɔ Panin no kyerɛɛ sɛ ɔnhwɛ GLC no anim, ɛno yɛ nea ɔtwerɛtwerɛ no so, enti ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde bɛyɛ Ayine kɔɔ ne "court" no sɛ ɔbɛyɛ adwuma. Owura Ndebugre seɛ, saa nsɛm yi nyinaa ara na ɛnte sɛ wɔn a ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ no yɛ robɔt, enti ɛremma wɔn nnya nsɛm a ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ no kakra.
Ɔhyɛɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu asoafoɔ a wabu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie hɔ no, wɔka sɛ, "wɔn a wɔnnyɛ wɔn nkyerɛ wɔn asɛm anaa wɔn ntwerɛ nsɛm. Sɛ wodi bɔ sɛ mmarahyɛbadwafoɔ nyɛ ɛmmɔne sɛ wɔn nhwehwɛmu a, ɛbɛsan wo de w’adwene besi so?
“Merennye nni sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin no nnyɛ nokware anaa mmara Kwaadubɔfoɔ no.
Menka sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin a ɔda Asoeɛ no ano adesoɔ sɛ ɔmfa Kwan mu no nti, sɛdeɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔbɔ asɛnnibea ano ɛnti ɔmfa asɛnnibea ho nti ɔwɔ sɛ ɔbɔ asɛnnibea ano ɛna ɔwɔ sɔhwɛ mu.
Nsɔhwɛ sɛ kwaadubɔfoɔ no gyina sɛ woagyina asɛm a wode hyɛ daakye no nti, ɛsɛ sɛ wobɛkɔ hɔ na wɔde nsɛntwerɛfoɔ a ɔdeda wɔn press conference ne so nti, na afei de asɛm no bedi dwuma.
Ƹrentumi mma wo ho ba hɔ na sɛ ɛkɔfa biasɛm a ɛho hia paa a, wobɛtumi anya complaining nanso m’adwene yɛ wɔn sɛ, ɛyɛ premature na mɛtu Ayine sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Amorisɛm Asoeɛ no bɛtɔ nea ɛwɔ sɛ ɔyɛ asɛm no nyinaa, ɛyɛ wɔn ho sɛ wɔbɛsan akɔ asɛm panin no annyɛ adwuma"
Ekuo a ɛhwɛ ɔman no mu National Peace Council (NPC) ahyɛ measures kɔ ase sɛ ɔbɛpae ɔman no anim de tackling the polarisation a ɛwɔ man no anim wɔ afe a atwa mu no ano.
Sɛdeɛ amanyɔkuo no kyerɛ no, amanyɔkuo a ɛmu da hɔ yɛ amanyɔsɛm mu ɛha amanyɔsɛm no ahyɛ aseɛ nti ɛho abɛhia sɛ wɔn nipɛ ananmu.
NPC kaa asɛm yi wɔ adanefoɔ ne amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ a wɔwɔ Ada a ɛwɔ Nkran Mantam mu.
Commonwealth Secretariat ne United Nations Development Programme (UNDP) na wɔahyɛ aseɛ wɔ Ghana abatoɔ nhyehyɛeɛ aseɛ.
Ná ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ kyɛfa wɔ asɛnnibea ho dwuma no bɛnya amanyɛsɛm mu asɛm asomdwoeɛ, amanyɔkuo tolerance, asomdwoeɛ ne ɔmanbuo na ɔman no kankɔ.
Nnipa a wɔdii Commonwealth Secretariat yi no ne ɔtwerɛtwerɛni panin, Dr. Angela Lusigi; ɔmanpanin a ɔda Scotland ano, Owura Kojo Oppong Nkrumah; the Interior, Owura Ambrose Dery ne National Security, Owura Albert Kan-Dapaah.
Nnipa panin a ɔwɔ Electoral Commission, Dr Eric Bossman Asare; apolisifoɔ a ɔhwɛ Inspector-General of Police, some executive members of the National Democratic Congress, the New Patriotic Party, the Convention People's Party, faith-based organisations, traditional rulers ne civil society organisations.
Owura Dery kaa sɛ nnipa aban dwumadie a wɔde wɔn nhyehyɛeɛ so wɔ December abatoɔ mu no, anhwɛ a ɛde nsɛnnennen bɛsi n’anim yi na ɛde bɛboro nnipa baesie.
Ɔkaa sɛ asɛm a polisifoɔ de asɛm 32 na asɛe koraa wɔ mmeamea nyinaa ara akyi wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Owura Dery kaa sɛ aban asi n'ani so sɛ ɔmma wɔn a wɔde saa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ yi kwaadubɔfoɔ.
Owura Kan-Dapaah kaa sɛ amanyɔsɛm mu tolerance ne consensus building nso ayɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ ɔman no mu amanyɔsɛm mu asomdwoeɛ ne amanyɔsɛm mu asomdwoeɛ.
Rt Hon. Scotland bɔɔ Ghana manfoɔ aba so wɔ asomdwoeɛ a ɔde wɔn nhyehyɛeɛ so kasaa wɔ ɔman no mu, a ɔkae sɛ ɔnyɛɛ Commonwealth family pa.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, Ghana abɛyɛ man no deɛ wɔ democracy mu, a ɛka sɛ "ɛyɛ awɔ asoafoɔ wɔn aso mu, nanso ɛyɛ ɔhaw a amanfoɔ no deɛ. Yɛwɔ hehwɛ na yɛboaa Ghana anim.
Ɔkɔɔ so kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔnyɛ nnipa a wɔatwa wɔn ho ahyia ɛne mmabunu ne wɔn mma mu wɔ ɔman yi mu.
NPC panin paa, Ɔbenfo Dr Ernest Adu-Gyamfi kaa sɛ n’asoeɛ no reyɛ adwumakuo a ɛbɛma amanyɔsɛm akɔ so de ɔne amanyɔkuo akɛseɛ wɔ abatoɔ mu na amanyɔkuo akɛseɛ wɔ abatoɔ mu.
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ, asɛm a ɔkaae wɔ 2020 abatoɔ no mu no bɛboa ma woundwen woundwen ɔko a ɛkɔ so wɔ berɛ a atwa mu no.
Kwankyerɛfoɔ Panin a ɔda Transeco Minerals ne Mining ano, Owura Godwin Amarh de akuma abɔ sukuu adan nsia wɔ Akyem Ampapatia a ɛwɔ Atiwa Atifi Mantam a ɛwɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu
Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a wɔde di dwuma yɛ cedi mpem aha nnwɔtwe na yɛ ka akyire Ɔpepem Baako akyire Ɔpepem Aduonum. (CSR)
Ɔrekasa wɔ dan no mu no, Owura Amarh kyerɛɛ sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔbɛma adesua bɛkɔ so ama mmofra a wɔn ho ntotoeɛ no ayɛ mmerɛ ama wɔn ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛma wɔanya suban pa wɔ nwomasua mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ adesua bɛko so wɔ ɔman yi mu abɛhia sɛ ɔbɛsi nwomasua nkankɔ nti, heni nea enti a n’adwumakuw no pɛ sɛ onya nwomasua mu.
“Yɛn a wɔwɔ Transeco Mining ne Fagutubea Adwuma no sii gyinaeɛ sɛ ɛbɛboa ama mmofra a yɛwɔ yɛn adwuma no bɛnya nhyehyɛeɛ a adekyerɛ ne adekyerɛ kɔ so wɔ mfitiaseɛ no mu. Yei nti na yɛhwɛ sɛ yɛyɛ education titiriw wɔ yɛn corporate social responsibility mu.”
M’ani gye ho sɛ mebaa sukuu yi firi Ampapatia sukuu mu hɔ. Yɛn nyinaa nim sɛ adesua a ɛwɔ nwomasua ho abɛhia paa na ɛbɛma asuafoɔ a ɛwɔ sukuu mu no anya nwomasua pa. wɔ sɛ wɔbɛsua adesuafoɔ ama wɔn ho anya nwomasua pa ɛno nti na yɛde sakre sakre sakre yi yɛɛ saa Kindergarten no mu.”
Owura Amarh kaa sɛ sukuu yi nso yɛ Ampapatia adwumakuo panin a ɔwɔ ɔman no anim anya nkitahodie sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ wɔn dwumadie ase firisɛ wɔn aseɛ wɔ mpɔtam hɔ no.
Anokwasɛm ne nsɛmmɔne a ɛfiri sɛ aban de banbɔ fagudeɛtu nnwuma wɔ ɔman no mu no, Owura Amarh debunked nsɛm a ɛyɛ nwanwa so na kyerɛɛ sɛ ɛyɛ nnipa sɛ wɔde tu fagudeɛ ano na ɛnyɛ yiye.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, aban abɔ nneɛma foforɔ a ɛfa fagudeɛtu anamɔn, nhyehyɛeɛ ne nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfa fagudeɛtu anamɔn na ɛnyɛ deɛ ɛso.
“Banbɔɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ banbɔ fagudeɛtufoɔ nsɛmmɔne wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ ne kwaeɛ mu sɛ ɛbɛyɛ adwuma a ɔman no banbɔ mu. Enti nea aban no reka ne sɛ ɔbɛyɛ ama fagudeɛtufoɔ nnwuma akɔ nkankɔ wɔ ɔman no mmara mu.” Owura Amarh kaa sɛ.
Ne sei nti na ɔtu fagudeɛtufoɔ fo sɛ wɔn nkɔ adwuma nanso ensure sɛ wɔbɛyɛ wɔ mmeaeɛ a ɛho hia.
Owura Amarh ne Ghanaman Association of Small Scale Miners (GNASSM) se nkurɔfoɔ no bɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔn adwene nhyehyɛeɛ yɛ mma a wɔde wɔn concession no ho adwene.
Ɔkae sɛ fagudeɛtufoɔ a wɔyɛ nneɛma no yɛ adwuma sɛ wɔnnyɛ nsawɔsoɔ a ɛmma wɔn nnyinasoɔ na wɔmma wɔn nsa akyigye.
Ɔkaa sɛ nnipa a agye fagudeɛtufoɔ no nsii saa ansa na wɔretu fagudeɛ no, nanso ɛsɛ sɛ wɔredi nneɛma bebree hɔ.
“Yɛn adwumayɛfoɔ employa nnipa dodoɔ a wɔwɔ communities mu. Yɛsɛ sɛ yɛn adwuma yɛ adwuma pa ara na ɛbɛma yɛn nnipa no da so adi dwuma. Menim ebinom a wɔwɔ sukuu mu na ebinom nso ama nkura ase sɛ yɛbɛte fagudeɛtufoɔ a ɛte saa nneyɛɛ nneɛma a ɛbɛma fagudeɛtufoɔ no bɛsɔ ani.”
Rebecca Foundation asɛm anya Memorandum of Understanding (MoU) with the Abdul Samad Rabiu Africa Initiative (ASR Africa) wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe($500,000).
Yɛde grant no bɛgye ASR Africa sika a ɛyɛ Africa Fund for Social Development ne Renewal na wɔde boaa Rebecca Foundation nwomasua dwumadie no.
Berɛ a wɔrekasa no anim no, Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ Panin a ɔda ASR Africa ano, Owura Ubon Udoh bɔɔ Ghana maame a ɔde ne ho bɛhyɛ nkwadaa no mu firii asomdwoeɛ ne mmofra wɔ ɔman no mu.
Ɔsan nso hyɛɛ nkwadaa a wɔhwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ma amammuo ka nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛboa amammuo no akɔ soro na akɔseɛ a ɛboa amammuo no ntam wɔ nnua, apɔmuden ne mmeɛnsa sikasɛm mu.
"Yɛyɛɛ yɛn sukuu dwumadie na yɛhunuu sɛ Rebecca Foundation yɛkuo a ɛwɔ Ghana na ɛmaa ASR Africa bɔɔ sɛ wɔboa yɛn Rebecca Foundation nnwuma.”
Executive Director a ɔda Foundation no ano, Mrs. Rebecca Akufo-Addo de anigyeɛ maa ASR Africa sɛ wɔboaa no ma foundation no.
Ɔbɔɔ ahyehyɛeɛ a wɔyɛɛ foundation no sɛ wɔnhyɛ saa agyinaeɛ yi ma mmofra a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu bɛdi dwuma wɔ ɔman no mu.
UKfoɔ asi nnyinasoɔ wɔ asien a ɛrekɔ so wɔ arrest ne wɔn aseɛ Nnamdi Kanu a ɔyɛ nneyɔeɛ bi a ɔredi nneyɔeɛ a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ɔman yi mu wɔ Nigeria atɔeɛ mantam mu a etni Igbofo dodoɔ no bɔɔ wɔn animtiaa.
Atɔtorɛ general kyerɛ sɛ Owura Kanu a wadi mfeɛ aduonu nsia wɔ Sunday with the help of Interpol na flown kɔɔ Nigeria.
Ɔ face treason-related charges wɔ Nigeria nanso ɔbɔɔ ɔman no mu afe 2017 while wɔ sika a na bail no mu.
Akyinnyegyeɛ bi sɛ ɔbɛka no wɔ UK, a wosusuw sɛ ɔyɛɛ basaa wɔn a wobetumi de agu.
Yɛbɛka sɛ, “Yɛhunuu sɛ Nnamdi Kanu kɔɔ wɔ UK sɛ ɔne yɛn nhwehwɛmu kwan a ɛfa wɔn extradition purposes,’’ British Soafoɔ panin bi ka kyerɛɛ BBC.
Nigeria’sɛmmubea apolisifoɔ anya nteteeɛ yi wɔ Benada.
Wɔkyere no, wɔbɛwie awerɛhow no ase Ayɛwohomumɔ 26 July.
Wɔn a wadi mfeɛ aduonu num no bɛyiyi ɔhaw firi 2009 mu aberɛ a ɔyiee Radio Biafra wɔ Nigeria firi London, using the platform to call for Biafran independence na ɔhyɛɛ nkurɔfoɔ sɛ wawu ɔno nneyɛeɛ a Nigeriaman no amfa arms.
Ɔpepem mmienu akyi no, na ɔhuu Abifra Nnipa dodoɔ a wɔyɛ Biafra (Ipob) a na Nigeria authorities kaeɛ sɛ ɔyɛ nnipa bi a wɔnnyɛ bi wɔ man no mu.

Institute of Directors-Ghana (IoD-Gh) akɔhyɛ Ghana Sikakorabea Kɛseɛ (BoG) aba so wɔ ɔman no mu sɛ ɔnam akɔyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ papa wɔ ɔman no mu.
Ƹsan nso ahyɛ nkwadaa yi ne sikakorabea kyerɛ sɛ wɔn ne sikakorabea no bɛboa ama adwumakuo nnwuma atu mpɔn wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Berɛ a asaanodwuma yi kyerɛɛ institute a ɛhwɛ BoG no, Ɔpanin a ɔda IoD-Gh ano, Owura Rockson Kwesi Dogbegah, eulogisedɔ manpanin a ɔda sikakorabea kɛseɛ ano, Dr Ernest Addison, sɛ waboa ama ɔpanyin paa wɔ sikasɛm nkorabata mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, BoG a ɛdii kan a Dr. Addison dii kan no maa sikakorabea nnwuma a yɛbɛfa so atɔ yɛn sikasɛm nkorabata.
Krataa a wɔwɔ institute no kaa sɛ wɔn nhyiamu no yɛ sɛ wɔbɛsesa sikakorabea no ama yayi akwannya so wɔ ɛkanyan ntotoeɛ a ɛhwɛ nkɔsoɔ a ɛbɛboa ama adwumayɛ akɔ so wɔ Ghana na seekye nkanim a ɛfa BoG ne institute ntam.
Ɔrekasa afa IoD-Gh dwumadie no ho no, Owura Dogbegah kaa sɛ, wɔn a wɔyɛɛ IoD-Gh dwumadie no daa adi dwuma a ɛyi sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ ama adwumayɛ akɔ soro wɔ Ghana manfoɔ.
Ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ sikasɛm mu mpuntuo nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ sɛ aban nhyehyɛeɛ yi bɛdi dwuma a wɔde bɛhyɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi adane wɔn sɛ wɔbɛsi corporate governance excellence awards dabiara wɔ suapɔn a wɔyɛ dwadie mu sɛ wɔde bɛdi ɔhaw a ɛyɛ ankorɛankorɛ ne adwumakuo nnwumakuo a wɔwɔ ɔman yi mu na wɔnam akwannya pa a wɔde reboa Ghana sikasɛm mpuntuo nso.
Ɔkaa sɛ Institute ne adwumakuo a ɛwɔ wɔn ne wɔn a wɔhwɛ akwannya adwuma no bɔɔ Ghana Association of Integrated Thinking and Reporting nkabom a ɛfa nsianisɛeɛ ne sustainable way of value creation ne reporting a wɔhyiaa nnwumakuo ahodoɔ.
Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ kaa sɛ, wɔn a wɔyɛ sikasɛm ho nimdeɛ akɔ soro paa wɔ sikasɛm nkorabata mu.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, sikasɛm mu nhwehwɛmu, akwannya korɔno, ɔne shareholder behaviour ne related-party transactional breaches ɛka ɛne ɛmmoa a ɛkɔɔ so na akɔgyina sikakorabea bi wɔ sikasɛm mu ne wɔn consequent resolution.
Ɔsii so dua sɛ asomdwoeɛ biara nni hɔ a Ghanakuo mpɛ sɛ wɔbɛdi boa sikasɛm asoeɛ na wɔbɔɔ asoeɛ no sɛ ɔmfa sikakorabea adwuma no nnyɛ asɛm pa ara wɔ Ghana sikasɛm nkorabata mu.
Arteta ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde bɛdɔ afe a etwaam no.
Asɛm no akyi no, Arsenal pɛ sɛ wɔnkɔ Mikel Arteta na bɔɔlbɔkuo no nso akan back him sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ Gunners mu afe a etwaam no.
Biribiara nni hɔ a wɔbetumi ayɛ den sɛ Arsenal gyinaeɛ akyi nanso bɔɔlbɔkuo no pɛ sɛ wɔbɛka wɔn ahyɛ bɔɔ mu mmɔden.
Serious asɛmfua bebree rebisa wɔn a wɔyɛ maame anaa ɔne dressing room no bɔɔlbɔkuo no ho mmuae sɛ ɔyɛ man panyin a wɔwɔ adwuma no.
“Nanso na Arteta a wadi mfeɛ 39 atwam no, wɔn nimdeɛ a ɛwɔ Pep Guardiola sɛnea ɔyɛ anika.”
Nteeɛ ne sɛ, berɛ a na ɔhyɛɛ Arsenal mfeɛ aduonu nsia atwa mu no, na wogye di sɛ wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo no ngyinasoɔ mmiɛnsa ne Unai Emery, ne man a ɔhyɛɛ ne a wɔde bɔ Europa League mu.
Arteta firi bɔɔlbɔ Arsenal na wɔayi akansie mmiɛnsa ama wɔn a wɔhwɛ sɛ wɔpere bɔɔlbɔkuo no akansie nanso sɛ wɔhwɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo no a, ɛreyɛ den na wɔhwɛ Chelsea ne Tottenham akyi kɔɔ bebree further ahead.

Nanso metena ka sɛ, “Nnipa a wɔwɔ Kroenke adwuma no ntumi nna ka.”
ɛyɛ a Arteta de n’adwene reyɛ bridges, bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtumi ayɛ wɔn mma wɔn tactics mu na wɔnam n’ano aba asɔ berɛ a na wɔatoto abaasɛm no abaasɛm a ɛbɛyɛ den ama wɔn ahyɛ aseɛ.
De Gea mpɛ sɛ ɔka No2
Manchester United bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɔdaa goolu ne David De Gea dii kan kɔɔ fam aberɛ a wɔɔhyɛɛ aseɛ afe 2023 ɔne ne agents no testing the waters to see which clubs behyɛ a ɔbɛhyɛ aseɛ wɔn mma no.
“Matete sɛn nea ɔbaa sukuu yi mu inside Old Trafford so sɛ mmerɛ a Dean Henderson ne Owura De Gea annyɛ wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu mpɛn dodoɔ bio.”
Mepɛ sɛ menya nkitahodie afiri Atletico Madrid, Paris Saint Germain ne Real Madrid hɔ.
Mfe mmienu a atwam no, na wadi mfeɛ aduonu nsia akyi wɔ ne bɔɔlbɔkuo yi mu ɛnam so ɛbaa kuo no gye di sɛ wadi mfeɛ mmienu no atu mpɔn.
Manager Solskjaer kaa sɛ, “Gyaafoɔ a wɔhwɛ goalkeeper nnwuma no yɛ adeɛ knit group.
Wɔ adwumam ho ntɔkwa no, wɔhyehyɛ dwumadie a wɔde bɛkɔ soro no, wɔhyehyɛ ahodoɔ no mu, individual sessions a wɔadi yɛ no, na wɔn nso twerɛ yɛn ho bio.
baa saa a, ɛte baa goalkeka ne botaeɛ nnwuma no top.
yɛ anika ketewaa biara.
M’ani gye di sɛ kwan a ɔtu anamɔn no yɛ De Gea tirim no sika a ɔde ne tɔɔ ne shirt no mu na ɔhyɛɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu aberɛ a ɔrekɔhyɛ goal ho ansa na ɔtu akɔhyɛ goal mu. Ayɛ yie sɛ ɔbɛkɔɔ Old Trafford mu.
Mede bɔne West Brom kɔn ase biara
Premier League mmienu a yɛatoto wɔlbɔkuo West Bromwich Albion.
Apira a ɛkyerɛ sɛ yetwam a ɔounce back from the Championship no bɛyɛ sɛ ɔbɛkɔ manager Sam Allardyce bɛsua sɛ ɔne no ankasa bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu.
Ɔyɛɛ yaw sɛ n’ani bɔɔ ne din biara sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo biara ɛna bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛwɔ West Brom no n’adwuma akɔ sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ no.
Ainsley Maitland-Niles, Conor Gallagher ne Okay Yokuslu bɛduru wɔn a wɔyɛ wɔn parent clubs mu berɛ a na wɔrehuru no nanso Matheus Pereira, Callum Robinson, Hal Robson-Kanu ne Karlan Grant bɛtumi ayɛ wɔn ani wɔ lower league mu.
Ɔbarima a ɔwɔ City
Who ne bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛyɛ Manchester City dii mu no?
No, ɛnyɛ Raheem Sterling.
Manager Pep Guardiola hyɛɛ bɔɔlobɔ bi aseɛ, na ɛsɛ sɛ obiara a ɔhyɛɛ bɔɔlobɔ no mu de atɔ ɔhaw 10 yard.
Akwan pii wɔ City squad mu nanso Gabriel Jesus bɔɔ nea ɔyɛ ntɛm paa.

Thomas Tuchel beaeɛ wɔ fagudeɛtu a ɛresɛe Kai Havertz na ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔka ne mmiɛnsa a ɛtɔ so mmienu yi awieɛ wɔ Fulham.
Tuchel kyerɛɛ sɛ ɛnnɛ na Kai anɔpa Stamford Bridge a ɛwɔ Bayer Leverkusen no ɔkwan bi so no ɔnnɛ na ɛnyɛ papa.
Moving fi amanɔne ɔman mu no, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔhyehyɛ mmara sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɔbea no nketenkete no, nanso ɔmpɛ sɛ Covid-19 na ɔhwehwɛ ne ho ase.
Akannii bɔɔlbɔkuo yi akan wɔ Champions League final ne akyi akansie no, Tuchel gye di sɛ, bɔɔlbɔkuo no bɛtɔ nea ɔde bɛhyɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu.
Solskjaer isurui bɔɔlbɔkuo United kɔɔ ɔnim bio
Manchester United bɛtumi akɔ Manchesterfoɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ no actively showing aggression towards theɔsɛm akɔ mu nanso inside the bɔɔlbɔ no adane nyinaa adi sɛ wɔn bɛyɛ suban pa, na wɔn anya nsunsuansoɔ biara nni hɔ a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ.
Ɔpanin a ɔda United adwumayɛfoɔ yi ano ne Ole Gunner Solskjaer, na ɔne abusuafoɔ a wɔn di ɔsram yi mu no, obiara kyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mpena sɛ wɔbɛdɔ United adwuma so wɔ berɛ a atwa mu yi mu.
Solskjaer bɔɔeɛ ɔkwan a United dii kan kɔɔ maa Bruno Fernandes ne Edinson Cavani na both ahyɛɛ bɔne a ɛka ho aberɛ a Manchester dii mu.
Cavani ahyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ɔreyɛ ama afe foforɔ yi mu na ɛyɛ ne belief ne Solskjaer hwee a ɔsuaa no.
Paul Pogba te nka sɛ wabrɛ ne ho ase, na n’adwuma manager no reyɛ adwuma.
Sɛ United dii nkunim wɔ akansie bɔɔ mu a, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔfa back up, ɔkasa, na more often than not wɔn awiei.
wom nneɛma biako a wɔde thank out-going Executive Vice-Chairman Ed Woodward for and that ɛmaa Solskjaer bɛtumi ayɛ wɔ adwuma no mu, survive ɔhaw a ɛyɛ den na ama ne bɔɔlbɔkuo no ayɛ ɔhaw pii.
“Sɔskjaer yi ho hia paa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ Unitedfoɔ ne wɔn a wɔyɛ fango wɔn di nsawɔsoɔ na wɔn a wɔka kyerɛ wɔn sɛ yei yɛ berɛ a atwa mu no.”

Ndlovu ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛho abɛhia sɛ wɔmfa mmara ho nhyehyɛeɛ yi nkɔ so mfeɛ aduonu baako pɛ. Ɔkaa sɛ mmara no ɛsɛ sɛ wɔmfa mmara foforɔ a ɛbɛma aboro a ɛkɔ akyiri a ɛbɛma amono.
Ndlovu kaa sɛ ɛmfɛm bi te sɛ mental illness, HIV / AIDS anaa disability were ɛne ɛmfɛm bi a wɔbetumi agyina hɔ sɛ wobetumi ato hɔ.
Ndlovu kyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmara no ɛnyɛ ɛmma banbɔ ama ayaresabea wɔn ho a ɛmfata sɛ wɔn anaa dɔkotafoɔ bɛyɛ ɔwofoɔ ama ayaresabea nkontaa ntɛm.

Zimbabwefo bi wɔ ɔman bi so no ka sɛ wɔnkutoo wɔ ɔman no mu firisɛ Robert Mugabe a ɔyɛ kuw bi nti ɔmfa Kwan mu no na wɔka kyerɛ wɔn.

Wɔka sɛ ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔn ne aban nnwuma ahodoɔ na aka wɔn ho no yɛ ɛfiri sɛ ɛnyɛ transportation kakraa biara, ɛne sɛ wɔn aban nnwuma no daa wɔn nsa asomdwoeɛ, biom nso enni aban kakraa bi a wɔde wɔn daa wɔn nsa ama wɔn.

Wɔ nnawɔtwe mmienu no mu no, wɔbɛyɛ nnipa mpem ɔha ne aduowɔtwe na corona virus nso rekɔ mu wɔ ɔman no mu mpem ɔha ne aduowɔtwe na yareɛ no ara wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa.

Wɔkaaɛ sɛ Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔda nsɛntwerɛfoɔ ano, Ms. Monica Mutsvangwa buaa nsɛnkyerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ase.

Ɔdeɛ ɛkyerɛɛ nea enti a wansii so dua sɛ wɔbɛkɔ asɛm about Mugabe funeral no, Mutsvangwa ne Fango Soafoɔ Sibusiso Moyo kaa sɛ ɛyɛ nwanwa sɛ ɔbɛtwe ne nhyiamu a na Mugabe n'abusuafoɔ a wɔwɔ Singapore no na wakɔɔ ɔman no mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ aban ne Ɔmanpanin Mugabe abusua no reyɛ adwuma.
Mprenpren mu no, King Katizagombo panin, Gibson Jenami kaa sɛ ɛnyɛ nsɛm a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Mugabe aseɛ berɛ a aban, led by Emmerson Mnangagwa ne baasa no na ɛredi saa kwan no.
Mprenpren mu no, Ɔpanin a watwa mu no, Major General Trust Mugoba a wadi mfeɛ aduonu nsia last week no bɛdaa no adi wɔ Heroes Acre burial ground a ɛwɔ Harare no.

Moyo kaa sɛ aban no yɛɛ planning sɛ ɔbɛde atikyafoɔ no kɔɔ wɔn ho mma wɔn.
Aban no kyerɛɛ sɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ, a ɛnsɛ sɛ dɔkotafoɔ, wɔnnyaa bosea 60 de wɔn mu, na nnɛ nhyiamu a wabɔ mu no sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ama apɔmuden ne sikasɛm ho asoeɛ no akɔ ntam sɛ ɔbɛyɛ apii ama adwumayɛfoɔ no.
Apɔmuden Soafoɔ, Dr Obadiah Moyo a ɔkaa sɛ ɔbɛtwe ne sikasɛm asoeɛ nkra sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ama abɛbuo no ano mpɔn pii.
Wɔnna adwumam no, wɔnna ɔtetena no bɔɔ sɛ wɔn sika dodoɔ no yɛ adeɛ so.
Ekuo a wɔredi apam sɛ wɔbɛkae nnipa a wodi mmara ho adwumayɛfoɔ a yɛfrɛ no Occupy Africa Unity Square panin, Itai Dzamara, the ɛyɛ Dzamara Trust, nnɛ celebrated International Women Day.
Dwumadie no kɔɔ so wɔ Highfield beaeɛ a ɛmaa ɛmmaayea ne mmaa a wɔdii dwumadie no wɔ berɛ a wɔde amena ahoɔdenbɔ no sanitary pads ne more.
Berɛ a ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ ma Dzamara family a ɛwɔ Itai Dzamara adwumakuo no ho, Owura Partson Dzamara ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɔreyɛ adwene sɛ ɔbɛboa nnipa mmienu yi wɔ ɔsram yi mu berɛ a na ɔrekɔ so wɔ berɛ a ne brother Itai awu fi bere a atwam no.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ ne n’abɛdiakyire wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu ne nsɛm mu human rights ne journalism ho nti ɔyɛɛ no mfasoɔ biara nti ɛtai Dzamara Trust no bɛba so yɛ deɛ ɛyɛ yaw ma no.
Ɔkaa sɛ n’adwuakuo yi adi dwumadie a wɔtete saa firisɛ ɛwɔ Highfields firisɛ ɛyɛ Itai bɔɔne nanso ɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔbɛkɔ mmara so na wɔn nimdeɛ ne osuahunu wɔ mmeɛnsa ne akyiri bi te sɛ mmara, nwomasua ne apɔmuden.
Nnipa a wɔda nnɛm yi ano ne Rememberance Zuze a ɔkae sɛ ɛwɔ mu sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na Owura Dzamara hɔ mpɛn pii no, n'ani gye ho sɛ ankorɛankorɛ a wɔyɛ wɔn asetena mu reyɛ adwuma.
Abaayewa bi a ɔbea no ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛnnɛ nsakraeɛ pii wɔ nnɛ.
Mprenpren mu no, Partson Dzamara abɔ amaneɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ nnipa mmienu a n’adamfo bi a ɔda n’anim wɔ Glen View no bɛkɔɔ Benada a ɛtɔ so wɔ Harare no.
Ɔkae sɛ saa kɔɔ so ara na wɔnhunu ne m’adamfo anaa sɛ wawu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ polisifoɔ, human rights activists, the Zimbabwe Human Rights Commission ne afoafoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔko a yɛfrɛ no Itai Dzamara dii nkɔmɔ wɔ dwumadie no mu.
Wiase a wiase di ɔhaw day, ɔbɛnem no, Zimbabwefo a wɔtete South Africa se ɛnyɛ nnyɛ biara de ɔbɛka ho sɛ South Africa ɔhaw no mfi hɔ.
Zimbabwefo binom ka sɛ, South Africa annyɛ wɔn a wɔhyia a wɔne organizations such as United Nations wɔ fa nnipa hodoɔ a wodi no ho kwan.
Ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin a ɔwɔ Zimbabwe Migrant Support Network ano, Shelton Chiyangwa ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ mmraafoɔ day ho hia mfasoɔ, nanso ɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛmia mmraa ahoɔden wɔ South Africa ho.
Chiyangwa kaa sɛ Zimbabwean abusua a wɔte South Africa no na nnipa dodoɔ no ara bio.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ n’adwumakuo no ne Zimbabwefoɔ ne amanɔne ahyɛ wɔn sɛ wɔbɛma wɔadi ntoasoɔ a ɛwɔ nkrataa mu.
Zimbabwe Exemption Permits vice-chairwoman Gladys Mangwende kaa sɛ n’adwumayɛfoɔ no dii nkɔmɔ wɔ nkɔsoɔ dwumadie mu nanso ɔhaw ne ho ban na mmom ɔyɛ nnipa bi ho asɛm.
Kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔda Human Rights Watch ano wɔ North Africa, Dewa Mavhinga se, adwumayɛ day ho yɛ important wɔ South Africa, berɛ a na Zimbabwefoɔ a ɛwɔ nkwadaa no mu yɛ adwuma.
Owura Mavhinga sii kyerɛɛ South Afrika Aban no sɛ ɔmfa mmara nkɔsoɔ no nyɛ adwuma.
Zimbabwean a George Manyika dii Mavhinga asɛm yi ase.
Gabriel Shumba, ɔpanin a ɔda Zimbabwe Exiles Forum ano, asrɛ United Nations, AU ne SADC sɛ wɔn nkɔmmɔ wɔ ɔhaw a yɛrefugeafoɔ refa mu no.
Lions nso hyɛɛ South Africa abɛdiakyire, Aaron Motseledi sɛ ɔnhyɛ n’asoeɛ mu ma ɔmma nnipa ho adwuma yɛ nnwuma sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛtumi anya adwuma.
Ɔhyɛɛ ankorɛankorɛ nnwumakuo ahodoɔ no sɛ wɔn ne n’adwumayɛfoɔ no bɛtɔ mmɔden wɔn nko ara.
Adwumayɛfoɔ no mu baako a yɛfrɛ no Francis Mukono kaa sɛ ɔrentumi nka sɛ refugee day na ɛhaw a ɛwɔ South Africa no nni emu yiye.
Ɔfoforɔ a ɔte hɔ no, Steven Chiweshe nso kaa sɛ nkogu ɛsɛ sɛ wɔagyae no.
Mandela Madumise, South Africa adwumayɛfoɔ panin paa a ɔwɔ nkrataa asoeɛ, kaa sɛ n'adwumayɛfoɔ no de United Nations Human Rights Council mmaa amfa mmoa a ɔreyɛ wɔn ho no ho nsɛm.
Madumise kaa sɛ aba a ɔsram yi mu a, n’asoeɛ no bɛhu nea ɛwɔ sɛ ɔyɛ de saa nsɛm yi ho.
Ƹyɛ awerɛhow sɛ, Zimbabwefoɔ bɛboro mpem mmeɛnsa ne Zimbabwefoɔ ahyɛ South Africa kɔɔ South Africa, accusing aban no sɔ ɔmfa Kwan mu.
Nanso Zimbabwe aban no se nnipa biare ahorow ahyɛ ɔman no mu de sɛ wɔbɛkɔ ɔman no afiri hɔ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ akwan pa.
Ayaresabea adwumayɛfoɔ, a wɔfrɛ no nsia ne dɔkotafoɔ a wogye n’anim no, awieɛ nnawɔtwe 33, seesei wɔn sika bɛyɛ enough ama wɔn adwuma mpo agu.
Akuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ ɔman yi mu no tense, na some ayɛ kɔɔ fie retwetwe wɔn ho a wɔde no treatment.
Akanneɛbɔ wɔ ayaresabea no bɛyɛ den sɛ Mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmmubea Adwumayɛfoɔ no adane no adi sɛ, sɛ sikasɛmmubea ne dɔkotafoɔ a wɔyɛ junior ne senior doctor no nsi wɔn ho a wɔbɛtoto wɔn no ho. Dɔkotafoɔ no Dr Aaron Musara ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nneɛma nkɔ yiye wɔ ayaresabea no mu.
Dr Musara kaa sɛ ɔkyerɛɛ aban sɛ ɔnhyɛ ne ho sɛ ɔbɛsesa nsɛm krataa bi a ɔde krataa fa akɔ so wɔ nnwuma mu no annyɛ nnyɛ biara.
Nnwumakuw a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ho abɛkɔ na wɔrenyɛ adwuma, na wɔreserɛ aban no sɛ ɔmfa wɔn US sika a wɔmaa wɔ Obubuo bosome wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe mu wɔ Obubuo bosome wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
Ɔpanin a ɔda Zimbabwe Nurses Association ano, ZINA, Enock Dongo se ɔman no nkasa yɛ goat'sɔ.
Dr. Tapiwa Mungofa a ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association (ZHDA) kyerɛɛ mu sɛ aban ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no ama wɔn anya oprehyɛn a ɛmma wɔn ntɛm.
Owura Mungofa kaa sɛ saa bere a mmofra nkumaa yi wenti yɛn ho no, wɔn mu no na wɔn ekuo kɔɔ fie gyinaeɛ a wɔhwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu ama COVID-19 a ɛmmoa wɔn ho no, wɔn na wɔn na wɔayɛ COVID-19 a ɛmmoa wɔn ho.
Wɔ Studio 7 mpɛn pii asua aban sisi asɛm a ɔde kasa tia apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ berɛ a na ɔyɛ apɔmuden dwumayɛni panin, Professor Amon Murwira twee ne ho ase aberɛ wɔ telefon so no.
Nanso berɛ a Owura Murwira de too dwa no, ɔde krataa ase ne nnyinasoɔ a ɔfrɛ no John Mangwiro de too dwa no anim ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ na wɔn adwene nhyɛ too kasa sɛ wɔbɛkasa.
Apɔmuden Asoeɛ Panin a ɔda Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ no ano, Dr. Paulinus Sikosana kaa sɛ wɔnnyɛ wɔn adwene wɔ COVID-19 yareɛ no mu na ɛnyɛ yiye sɛ ɔka nsɛm yɛn.
Apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ nso ka sɛ, sɛ aban yɛ adwuma mma adwumayɛfoɔ return to work na mmom ɛbɛma nsɛmmɔne a ɛmma wɔn ho dwiriw wɔn ho no a, ɛbɛboa ama ayaresa ɔman no afiri COVID-19 yadeɛ mu a nnipa 25 awu so ara.
Chinhoyi City Council se wɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ deɛ High Kɔɔto gyinaeɛ a ɛsii wɔn sɛ wɔn nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛtɔ so mmienu wɔ ɔman no mu.
Berɛ a ɔne adwadifoɔ a wɔn wiemhyɛn no rekasa wɔ nhyiamu a ɛda no so no, kuo no panin, Abel Gotora kaa sɛ wɔn bɛtɔ asɛm a ɛda kɔɔto no pɛ sɛ wɔn nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ a ɛda odwadifoɔ no ntam.
Nanso Owura Gotora kaa sɛ, banbɔ nhyehyɛeɛ no ntumi nkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛsi dan a ɛwahyehyɛ aseɛ no, nanso wɔn mma wɔn nsi dan a ɛhyɛ aseɛ nnipa baanu a wɔgyinaa kɔɔto no ho.
Tafadzwa Marimo, Emmanuel Ngwaru, Richard Svosve, Pepukayi Marega ne Devis Shopo na among those who took Chinhoyi kɔɔɔto.
Ɔbaa a ɔdi kan no mu a yɛfrɛ no Emmanuel Gwaru kaa sɛ ɔgyeɛ kɔɔto atɛmmuo no gye asɛm berɛ a aban no ka kyerɛɛ ɛdwa fie no sɛ ɔbɛsesa nnipa a yɛrebue dan no ama yatu mpɔn.
Owura Gwaru kaa sɛ nea ɔreka ne dodoɔ no ara ne sɛ ɛyɛ sika dodoɔ ma banbɔ no sɛdeɛ ɔbɛbue dan sie yi ama wɔn anya mpuntu dwumadie. Gadzema Councilor Patricia Chibaya kaa sɛ ɔmfa kɔɔto no asɛe sɛ berɛ a na ɔreyɛ nnipa dodoɔ yi afiri ɔman yi mu, nanso ɛnyɛɛ sɛ ɔbɛkyerɛɛ ɔmanfoɔ a ɔhwɛ anim wɔ mmeɛnsa yi nyinaa ara. wɔsan nso de kasa tiaa nnipa a wɔn di nsawɔsoɔ wɔ agye nsini no nyinaa ara.
Owura Gotora bɔɔ amaneɛ sɛ dansie yi bɛbue dan a ɛbɛnya nnipa 50 wɔ Gadzema sotɔɔ mu.
spokesperson for the Adwumakuo Zimbabwe Lawyers for Human Rights, Kumbirai Mafunda kaa sɛ, nnipa a wɔwɔ ma adwadifoɔ ho kwan sɛ wɔn dwumadie rehwehwɛ wɔn mmaranim ho kwan.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani dodow a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no regye nnwuma a wɔka sɛ wɔyɛɛ buee dan bi a na wɔaka ara.
Nanso traderfoɔ a ɛwɔ wiase no resi ɔhyɛɛ kɔɔto de wɔn dwumadie renyɛ.
Berɛ a ɔman Kɔɔto Baatan gyinaeɛ Benada sɛ ɔne nea ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde MDC amanyɔkuo no bɛdi Richard Morgan Tsvangirai House anaa Harvest House no.

Douglas Mwonzora a ɔsan yɛ amanyɔkuo no abɛdiakyire na ɔserɛ sɛ wɔn ne amanyɔkuo no panin wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu. Ɔsan nso gye sɛ amanyɔkuo no wɔ Makone ne Neil.
Nanso wɔka sɛ wɔn adwene nhyia wɔ wo so. Yɛn ntumi nnyaa Owura Makone ne Owura Niel nkrataa no ho dwuma.
MDC panin paa a ɔda MDC ano, Nelson Chamisa, Job Sikhala se St Marys area a ɛwɔ Chitungwiza ada birth toɔ nnipa a ɛresɛe amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ no sɛ ɔmfa mmoa wɔn ho na ɔmfa akɔ wɔn mmanoma.
Sikhala, a ɔyɛ Zengeza West Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no kaa sɛ ɔnsosɔeɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ polisifoɔ a ɔfrɛ no Jabangwe wɔ area no so sɛ ɔnkɔyɛ wɔn.
Yɛbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ yɛbɛfrɛ Owura Jabangwe nanso na ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔne yɛn mmuae.
Wɔ Studio7 nso ntumi nnyinaa nni hɔ a polisifo asɛm ani. Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi nti na ɛwɔ Studio7 sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ polisifoɔ nhwehwɛmu.
Nanso amanneɛbɔ kyerɛ sɛ ɛsiane MDC amanyɔkuo no asɛm no yɛ ɔde amanyɔkuo no akɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ Sikhala a wadi mfeɛ aduonu nsia wɔ Asoeɛ Baatan no soboɔ sɛ ɔnam soboɔ a ɛtu Emmerson Mnangagwa akyi no so ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nnipa pii wɔ hɔ a wɔmfa wɔn homesɔn.
Nnipa bɛboro 90 na wɔkɔɔto wɔn kaaeɛ wɔ Harare Fida a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa wɔ saa da no ara no.
MDC no pɛ sɛ ɔrekasa wɔ mmeaeɛ bebree a ɛwɔ mantam mu nanso polisifo no daeɛ a ɔde banbɔ Apam ano sɛ ɔmfa akwannyegyeɛ biara a ɛbɛma amanyɔkuo no agu.
Polisifoɔ abɔ Ghana sika kɔkɔɔ ma MDC wɔ Harare, Bulawayo, Gweru ne Masvingo so.
Animdefoɔ kyerɛ sɛ ebia wɔbɛkɔ so wɔ Mutare a MDC amanyɔkuo no de akɔ ɔtɔ so wɔ Yawoada no mu.
Kɔɔto Baatan no, Kɔɔto Baatan no atwe Ɔman Soafoɔ Ziyambi Ziyambi ne Finance Minister Mthuli Ncube sɛ wɔnnyi sika MDC-T a ɛtɔɔ Thokozani Khupe ne wɔn na wɔamentary budget law no adi.
Kɔɔto Baatan no, Ɔtɛmmuafoɔ Priscilla Munangati Manongwa gye too Yawda sɛ ɔtwee Ziyambi ne Ncube firi MDC-T faction, a ɛkyerɛ sɛ nea ɛwɔ sɛ wɔyɛ amanyɔkuo na fundɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu under mmarahyɛbɛdwafie (Finance) no.
ƆDC no de sika bɛyɛ R7,500 million wɔ RTGS mu.
Nhwehwɛmufoɔ kyerɛ sɛ Nelson Chamisa MDC hasɔ kɔɔto berɛ a na Ms. Khupe faction akɔyɛ adwuma wɔ sikakorabea bi a wɔhwɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ Chamisa mfidie no ho kwan sɛ nnipa a wɔrepɛ krado sɛ wɔbɔ sika wɔn steward Bank mu.
Chamisa MDC-T deputy spokesman, Luke Tamborinyoka kaa sɛ wɔn ani gye ne ho sɛ ɔbɛyɛ basaa.
Nanso Morgen Komichi a ɔte saa berɛ a onipa yi sɛ ɔnyɛ amanyɔkuo no kankɔ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ amanyɔkuo no Ɔman no Kɔɔto atɛmmuo a ɛgyinaeɛ sɛ mmara hyɛɛ ne nhyehyɛeɛ no mu sɛ ɔbɛyɛ ɔkandifoɔ amanyɔkuo no Ɔman no Kɔɔto no anim. Ɔkaa sɛ ɔbɛpɛ sika no sɛdeɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no panyin.
Nanso Owura Tamborinyoka kaa sɛ ɔwɔ sika no sɛee berɛ a MDC Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no wɔbuee mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu wɔ ne din.
Nanso Komichi kaa sɛ Owura Chamisa ne othersɛm nyɛ adwuma.
Mprenpren mu no, Harare mmaranimfoɔ Kudzai Kadzere kaa sɛ kɔɔto no agyinaeɛ bɛtumi atwe wɔn ho efiri nnansa yi mu.
Ziyambi ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 wɔ pono so sɛ wɔbɛyɛ wɔn krataa wɔ 10, sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ asɛm gyinaeɛ a Kɔɔto hyɛ no pɛ a, na wɔatwe wɔn krataa a ɛhyɛ kɔɔto no ase.
Yɛn ntumi nnyaa nkyerɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu, Jacob Mudenda anaa Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ Asoeɛ sɛ wɔn nwene nea ɔrekɔ so wɔ asɛm papers mu.
Nkabomfoɔ a wɔyɛ mmaranimfoɔ yi ka sɛ wɔn nhyɛɛ too dwa sɛ wɔmfa Chamisa MDC asɛm no ho nti, Kɔɔto no hyɛɛ wɔn a wɔhyɛ too dwa sɛ wɔbɛsan de sika no kɔɔ Chamisa MDC no ho.
“Nea ɛrenyɛ bere a MDC foforɔ agye saa sika yi ho.
Wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu, na ɔyɛ MDC panin paa, Welshman Ncube opposed Morgan Tsvangirai afe 2005 mu, na ɔde ne MDC mmienu no ahyɛ mmara mu, na ɔde n’ani bɛgyee MDC aban no biara, leaving Owura Tsvangirai, amammuo a ɛwɔ mmara mu no penny.
Another Zimbabwean, Dr Rita Nyampinga, a ɛwɔ Female Prisoners Support Trust a ɛwɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu nso kaa sɛ ɛyɛ ɔdɔ sɛ mmaayea nnipa mmienu yi atu afiri hɔ. Ɔkaa sɛ ɛyɛ wɔn sɛ wɔbɛgyee afiri hɔ 2020 International Women of Courage agyina.
Wɔde award yi kyerɛɛ mmarima a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa no, na United States Department of International Relations de ato dwa no.
Dr Nyampinga kaa sɛ ɛnnɛ na ɔpɛ sɛ odi saa anwummere yi ase, berɛ a na ɔyii wɔn ho sɛ ɔbɛgye nnipa 11 a wɔwɔ wiase afanan nyinaa.
Dr Nyampinga se wɔretu akwan kɔɔ mmeaeɛ a ɛwɔ United States no bɛsua sɛnea wɔn adwuma yɛ a, sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ a wɔrepɛ adwuma wɔ fie no bɛnya wɔn adwuma mu.
Dr Nyampinga se wɔn adwuma no gye ahobrɛase, na wɔn ani gye sɛ nkurɔfo ahwɛ adwuma a wɔreyɛ wɔ fie no ho.
Ɔrekasa wɔ saa dwumadie yi mu no, panin paa a ɔda ɔman no so, Michael Pompeo kaa sɛ, nkwadaa a ɔdaa mmra 12 wɔn no ho no yɛ nwanwa, na ɛsɛ sɛ wogye courage.
Dwumadie no ase mfeɛ aduonu num ni.
Wɔn a wɔmaa wɔn ho aka award yi ne Afghanistan, Armenia, Azerbaijan, Bolivia, Burkino Faso, Kazakhstan, Malaysia, Nicaragua, Pakistan, Syria, Yemen ne Zimbabwe.
Owura Pompey kaaɛ sɛ wɔn nhyehyɛeɛ ahodoɔ no yɛ deɛ ɛbɛboa ama mmeɛnsa anya adwuma wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa ara.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no no, Ɔman panin a ɔwɔ United States, Melania Trump kaa sɛ ɔreyɛ n’adwene sɛ mmaa ne fahodie nkɔanim a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa no.
Ɔkaa sɛ, ɛfiri sɛ wɔne mmaa a wɔayiyi wɔn din yi apem mfeɛ nyinaa akyi no, wɔn besua nnipa a wɔayiyi adwuma no ho dwuma wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa, efisɛ wɔn mu biara wɔn adwuma bɛyɛ adwuma wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔn mu bi yɛ adwuma wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa, nanso wɔanya so mfasoɔ.
Dr Nyampinga se ɔbɛyɛɛ mfeɛ aduonu mmienu sɛ ɔyɛ adebɔneyɛfoɔ 30 mmienu a atwam no.
Ƹnyɛ n’anim no, Ms Nyampinga yɛ adwumakuo a ɛwɔ Mmarahyɛ Badwam mu na wɔtoto Women Coalition Of Zimbabwe, Crisis In Zimbabwe Coalition, Women Academy on Political Leadership Excellence ne Women And Aids Support Network.

Banbɔ oprehyɛn a ɛda minibuses ne buses a ɛwɔ ZUPCO bus adwuma no ahyɛ ɔhaw no mu a ɛde akwansideɛ bebree ɛnam so ama nkurɔfoɔ anya Covid-19 yareɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu.
Nnipa bebree no ka sɛ, wɔn bebree asomdwoeɛ pii wɔ anɔpa a ɛkyɛn lɔɔre Kwan so a, ɛno na ɛma wɔn squeeze wɔn buses no mu.
Aban abɔdeɛ asɛm bi a ɛbɔ banbɔ kar sɛ ɔbɛmfa Kwan mu nnipa a wɔwɔ Covid-19 yadeɛ no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔmfa Kwan no nto hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yareɛ no biara nni dwuma, stating sɛ ɔbɛwie buses no na wɔmfa Kwan no nni dwuma.
Nanso wɔka sɛ, “Nteeɛ ne busubea nso wɔ ho sɛ wɔbɛgye saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi akyi, ɛne ɛsɛ sɛ ɛde ZUPCO delay in payment a ɛhyɛ aseɛ.”
Wɔ Dwoada no, na wɔn a wɔyɛ lɔɔre Kwan adwuma dawurubɔ dawurubɔ no bi ayɛ wɔn ho nhyiamu sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ a wɔresɛe wɔn bus no ho.
Benada no, wɔbɛhyɛ buses no sɛ wɔne aban ayɛfoɔ rebɛsi saa nsɛm yi ano reyɛ adwuma.
Studio 7 annye n’adwene sɛ ɔhwɛ ZUPCO wɔ deɛ pɛsɛmenkominya a ɛsi wɔn sɛ ɔbɛsi transport no so.

Lions se Aban no hwehwɛ sɛ ɔmma polisi, army anaa council police wɔ bus stops no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a mmara ɔbɛhwɛ ama wɔn anya nyarewa no ho ban.
Wɔsan ka sɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ ɛnkosi sɛ wɔn mmoa bustuari no mu hwɛ sɛ wɔnnyaa HIV anaa Covid-19.
Nnwuma a ɛwɔ Bulawayo wɔ akuo ahodoɔ a wɔwɔ kurow no mu akɔfa nsɛm ahorow a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛdeɛ nsuyiri kɛseɛ no ara na ɛsɛ sɛ aka.
Ɔpanin a ɔda Adwadifoɔ AbuZ ano (ABUZ) Victor Nyoni kaa sɛ nsuyiri yi adane wɔn nnwuma mu nti wɔn ekuo no hwehwɛɛ nsuo a ɛho hia paa sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ wɔn nsuo ase.
Owura Nyoni kaa sɛ ɔbɛma agyinatukuo a ɛwɔ banbɔ mu no sɛ ɔbɛpɛ sɛ wɔn nsu anɔw ɛnnawɔtwe a edi kan no mu.
Ɔkɔɔ so wɔ Bulawayo kurow mu no sɛ nsu yiri nnawɔtwe a ɛtɔ so mmienu ne aduonu baako akyi wɔ nsuo foforɔ a ɛhyɛ aseɛ sɛ wɔde rehye nsuo foforɔ a ɛwɔ Asoeɛ no.
Yei nso kaa sɛ nsuo no bebree a ɛso nkyerɛ sɛ nsuo no nni nsuo a Criterion ne Magwegwe nyinaa nsawɔsoɔ ma pumping nsuo.
Owura Nyoni se yɛnim sɛ ɔbɛyɛ te sɛ bulawayo kurow a ɛyɛ mfeɛ aduonu num a atwa mu no, ɛna nsuo ne nsuo mu pipe no yɛ dede.

Kwankyerɛfoɔ a wɔhwɛ dwumadie yi mu, Doctor Prince Butau kaa sɛ ɔredwene sɛ wɔbɛhehwɛ Owura Mnangagwa ɛbɛyɛ bi wɔ Yawoada anaa Dɛnkoro no.
Owura Mnangagwa a na ɔreyɛ adwuma no reba no ara na bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔn mma dɔkotafoɔ atuateɛ no rebɛsi wɔn.

“Saa ara nso na Owura Chiwenga firi ɔman yi mu kɔɔ ayaresabea wɔ South Africa, ɛwɔ Studio 7 nnim sɛ na ɔyɛɛ evidence sɛ ɔwɔ South Africa ayaresabea no.
Media soafoɔ Monica Mutsvangwa ne nsɛntwerɛfoɔ Nick Mangwana daa no adi asɛm yi aberɛ a Wɔne VOA Studio 7 wɔ Hare gyinaeɛ a ɔwɔ Zimbabwe sɛ wɔma wɔn arrest George Charamba.
Nanso Studio 7 amfa Charamba nhyehyɛeɛ sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ sɛ ebia na Chiwenga ill adi wɔ ayaresabea no.
Zimbabwean bi a yɛfrɛ no Carlos Chimbi ne ɔbarima bi a ɔwɔ Cape Town anim de akuma abɔ mu no.
Chimbi kaa sɛ ɔreyɛ n'ani sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ vice president no ama nnipa a ɛwɔ afie mu no ho kwan wɔ ɔman no mu berɛ a na ɔnhwɛ sɛ ɔbɛhia sɛ wɔkɔ medical treatment abroad sɛ wabrɛ ahwehwɛ no.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɔbɛyɛ n’ani sɛ ɔbɛma ne message akɔ ayaresabea no kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɔbaa a ayaresabea no ayaresabea asɛm kɛkɛ sɛ Owura Chiwenga ayɛ ayaresabea no ho nhwɛ, nanso ɔkae sɛ ɔhwehwɛ no anaa Owura Chiwenga nyɛɛ ayaresabea no ho.
Chimbi kaa sɛ ayaresabea no kɔkɔɔ no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ mmara no nni ngyinasoɔ a ɛmma no ho asɛm sɛ ɛbɛyɛ wɔn nko ara wɔ ayaresabea.

Tamborinyoka kaa sɛ nhyiamu yi nhyehyɛeɛ bebree no ɛbɛkɔ so ɔbɛkyerɛɛ sɛ MDCfoɔ no pɛɛ sɛ wɔn a wogye di wɔn ho sɛ ɔbɛbraa apolisifoɔ anaa wɔayi atikyafoɔ.

Wɔhwɛɛ Ahmed din wɔ ɔman no mu sɛ ɔde asomdwoeɛ bɛkɔ so wɔ ne amanehunu a atwam no mu no.
Ɔdi kan a obiaa a wɔdii kan wɔ award no mu ne Albert Luthuli of South Africa afe 1960.
Other awerɛhyɛn foforɔ a wɔde Nelson Mandela a ofi South Africa, Anwar Sedat a ɛwɔ Egypt ne Kofi Annan a ɔwɔ Ghana no ho.
Other winners a ɛka ho kyɛw ne, Archbishop Desmond Tutu ne Kenya manpanin Ellen Johnson Sirleaf na ɛyɛ Wangari Maathai a ɔyɛ ɔbea a ɛdi kan wɔ Abibirem Africa no mu.

Nneɛma bebree kɔ so wɔ Hwange National Park mu, na ɔma aban no adwene sɛ ɔbɛyɛ nnuan a ahoɔden wɔ pono no so.
Wɔ nsrahwɛ a yɛkɔɔ Studio7 wɔ Hwange National Park area no, yɛhunuu mmoawa a ɛdii kan bɔne mmoawa a wɔdii nnuaba wɔ afe yi mu.
Zimbabwe Parks ne Wildlife Management Authority (ZimParks) spokesperson Tinashe Farawo ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ, nnipa bɛyɛ duru ama elephants agye wɔn nsia wɔ ɔbɔ bosome wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe mu.

Sɛ nea ɛrenu no, wɔka sɛ ɔphant biako ne nnuan aduasa (200 L) na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde nnuan a ahoɔden (200 L) di dwuma.
Nanso seesei ZimParks no buu sɛ nnwumakuo nnipa mpem ahasa ne aduowɔtwe nnwɔtwe na wɔwɔ area no mu.
Nkabomkuo a ɛwɔ kuayɛ mu mpaninfoɔ binom se, ZimParks kyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛda wɔn ano yɛ nokware, na wɔka sɛ wɔreyɛ yɛ adwuma sɛ wɔbɛtɔ elephants mu.

Nanso Owura Farawo se nkurɔfoɔ a ɔkuru nneyɛɛ bi no nso keka sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ nnwuma a ɛwɔ abɔdeɛ mu no nnyɛ ɛfiri sɛ ɔphants ne nɔmoa ahodoɔ no ntumi nnya nkitahodie firisɛ ɔde n’adwumayɛfoɔ no da ayɛ adwuma ntɛm.

Wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduowɔtwe mu no, na Ngezi Platinum Stars a ɔwɔ Zimbabwe na ɛredi Caf Kuo no mu no, wɔyii bɔɔlobɔ afe baako mu berɛ a na wɔnhwɛɛ no Angolan Libolo so.
Wɔ afe 2015 mu no Harare City a wɔwɔ abrabɔ mu no na wɔdii kan wɔɔ Zanaco a ɔyɛ Zambia berɛ a na wɔdii kan ɔhyɛɛ 2-1 wɔ Rufaro Stadium na wɔdii kan ɔhyɛɛ ɔkuo 3-1 wɔ Zambia.

Deɛ tebea a ɛha no yɛ ne sɛ, FC Platinum wɔ nsakraeɛ pɔtee biara wɔ akansie mu no, wɔn ntumi mmienu ne nsakraeɛ wɔ akwan foforɔ mu, moreover, wɔn ahyɛ ɔsram ɔha aduonu nsia wɔ akwan foforɔ mu mmeɛnsa.
Asɛm no mu no, sɛ obiara bɛhyɛ bɔɔlobɔ mu wɔ Zimbabwe na wɔahyɛ saa wɔ Abibirem Africa no a, ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔman no mu nyɛ bɔɔlobɔ?

Na afe yi, FC Platinum hyɛɛ Gerald Takwara, Elvis Chipezeze ne Talent Chawapiwa wɔ afe yi mu, na afe yi hyɛɛ Rodwell Chinyafanere a ɔyɛ soccer star of the year trophy a wɔkɔɔ Baroka.
