Taylor kaa sɛ ɛhaw a ɛwɔ Manicaland no yɛ adeɛ pa ara sɛ Zimbabwe aban nnyɛ ɔwɔ mu biara nti.
Taylor, a ɔkɔɔ Manicaland ɔɔdwuma mu World Food Program helicopter no a ɔde ne ho yɛ adwuma no investing, ɔkaa sɛ ɛyɛ anika sɛ wɔhunuu sɛ aduan bɔne a ɛwɔ mantam no haw wɔ mantam no mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ mmofra a ɔte saa no nnya anigye. Ɔkaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ asɛm maa Manicaland manfoɔ no sɛ wɔnnyaa aduan ne ɔhaw yiye a, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔbɛboa wɔn ama wɔn annya composure.
Taylor nso kaa sɛ wɔn ntaa wɔ Chimanimani ne Chipinge wohu, na wɔn ntaafoɔ kae sɛ wɔn mmoa helpɛ ɛfiri amanyɔkuo a wɔwɔ amanyɔkuo no da.
USAID nso se wɔn nimdeɛ wɔ haw a wɔbɔ nkɔsoɔ ma Zimbabwefoɔ sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ kɔpem sɛ, nea ɛbɛyɛ a stormsɔre no nni baabi a wɔnhwɛ wɔn ho, ɛne nea wɔatumi ayɛ biara sɛ wɔbɛtumi akɔ atia ɔman no sikasɛm ntotoeɛ ho.
Esiane Cyclone Idai nsɛm no mu no, United States afa Zimbabwe nya sika ɔpepem ɔhapem 2.6 million.
Mprenpren mu no, Aban, United Nations ne Nnwumakuo a wɔhwɛ Apaadie so daa no adi sɛ, wɔde sika 60 million wɔ Cyclone Idai ase.
Nnipa bɛyɛ mpem ahasa aduosia wɔ Manicaland mantam mu, na ofi mu nnipa mpem aduasa nnwɔtwe na wɔn mu ayɛ mmofra.
Wɔ ntoasoɔ a ɛdi Cyclone Idai wɔ mansini no mu no, wɔasɛe adesuafoɔ 113 na wɔde wura nwomasua mu, na ɛ leaving adesuafoɔ a wɔn homeless.
Aban no se nnipa bɛyɛ 300 na wɔaka ahorow, na nnipa mpem ahanu baako na wowuwui wɔn no mu.
Yei kyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nnipa dodoɔ.

“Saa ara nso na Ms. Chindove kae sɛ ɔkɔɔ South Africa no yɛ adwuma sɛ ɛbɛyɛ a ɔrstɔe nni thirstɔe a n’anim wɔ nsu no mu.

Messi kaa asɛm yi aberɛ a wɔtaa Copa America akansie a ɛkɔɔ wɔ United States berɛ a na Argentina bɔɔ Chile mmɔden a ɛtɔ so mmienu no ama wɔn akyi wieɛ.
Wɔ Kwasida no, bere a Francisco Silva a Chile bɔɔ amaneɛ no too mu no, ɔrensii gyinaeɛ a yɛde bɔɔlbɔkuo no Sergio Romero kɔɔ nea ɔfa kwan no mu.

Fango adwumakuo a ɛwɔ Petrotrade se, sɛ aban reyɛ nneɛma boɔ sɛ wɔde toto ɛboɔ a wɔtɔn nko ara wɔ sika ho no mfasoɔ.
Berɛ a ɔmanpanin Petrotrade dwumadie panin Godfrey Ncube se ɛbɛyɛ sika a ɛbɛtumi de akɔ ma nnwuma no sɛ wɔbɛtɔ ama fango na wɔtɔ wɔn nko ara.
Owura Ncube gye too mu sɛ sɛ yɛato saa a, ɛbɛyɛ boɔ so gyinaeɛ nanso seesei ɔde wɔn nkuropɔn a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu aba asɛm no mu.
Owura Ncube kaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ aban ngye fann wɔ ɔman yi mu no yɛ fango adwadie nti na wɔanya bioma wɔ ɔtetena mu.
Owura Ncube kyerɛɛ sɛ wɔn bo ɛfiri ama fango a aban a wahyehyɛ no assistance wɔ dwumadie a ɔde too dwa no mu, ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ firi hɔ awieɛ no wɔn boɔ yɛ ɔpepem mmienu aduonu nan, nanso wɔɔ afe yi awieɛ no wɔn boɔ yɛ ɔpepem aduonu nan.

Ekuo a ɛhwɛ apaadie so no kaa sɛ ɔyɛ nwanwa sɛ mpuntuo nnwuma a ɛbɛkura ase wɔ ɔman yi mu no refa mu.
Zimbabwefoɔ wɔ Memenda da a ɛtɔ so mmienu yi mu kɔpem aduonu num akyi wɔ ɔman no afaanaa nyinaa, berɛ a na nnipa a wɔwɔ wɔn ho aka wɔn ho.
Ekuo a ɛhwɛ apaadie so no maa nnipa bebree keka sɛ wɔbɛyɛ aborɔfo ama wɔn anya white supremacy, nnipa bebree a wɔde awɔ wɔn suban no mu bebree sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ aborɔfo ama wɔn nyinaa totɔ wɔn suban no mu.
Nanso mfe 40 a atwam no ahyɛ aseɛ wɔ ɔman yi mu no, wɔkae sɛ nneɛma bi wɔ hɔ a, ɛnyɛ wɔn a wɔkae sɛ, ɛnyɛ wɔn nnwuma a wɔde bɛboa wɔn afie na wɔn nnwuma no ayɛ adwuma.

Apɔmuden nso wɔ ka sɛ, ɔhaw ahodoɔ no nyinaa akɔ so, berɛ a adan ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no regye nti.
Nnipa a few wɔn still working no ka sɛ, ɛtɔ da a wɔn ara deɛ ɛlɛtrɔnik mfiri mu yɛ den sɛ wɔbɛkɔ so ayɛ adwuma ama wɔn.
Wabɔ Ɔmanpanin a watwam Emmerson Mnangagwa a ɔde asraafoɔ abɛdiakyire wɔ 2017 mu, a na asraafoɔ panin a ɔwɔ maame Robert Mugabe ahyɛ aseɛ no ama ɔmanfoɔ abɛdiakyire hope for a brighterɛ ka.
Nanso wɔn mu biara no ayɛ ɔbɛyɛ ɔdɔkotafo ne ɔbɛyɛ ɔdɔkotafo, berɛ a na wɔka sɛ things are getting worse.
Nanso wɔ hɔ a ɛwɔ mfeɛ aduonu a atwam yi mu no, wɔn nnyɛ biara a Zanu PF atu saa mfeɛ yi aduasa mmienu yi?
Zanu PF panin a ɔwɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu mpaninfoɔ Regis Charumbira se n’abɛgyeɛ amanyɔkuo no dodoɔ ɔbɛpa a ɛmfa nnipa a wɔwɔ kurow no ho dwuma.
Owura Charumbira kaa sɛ n’asoeɛ no reyɛ nhwehwɛmu sɛ nnipa a wɔagye agye nneɛma yi ho bɛgye ne nsam, na ɛsɛ sɛ Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔn nkurɔfoɔ baabi a ɔwɔ fie no nyɛ Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔwɔ fie nyinaa mmom.

Wɔasrɛɛ IFP mmarahyɛbɛdwani sɛ wamfa banbɔfoɔ a wɔkura atuo wɔɔ ɔman yi mu wɔ bi aseɛ wɔ Thubalethu, Mthonjaneni (Melmoth) da a ɛtɔ so nnɔ.
Ɔkae sɛ, banbɔfoɔ a yɛfrɛ no Mayor a ɔkaa wɔn nnipa a wɔn ebinom ka kyerɛɛ ɔhaw bi a na ɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔn keserenee a ɛwɔ nkrataa no so no.
Ekuo mu baako no bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo no kankɔ wɔn ndie sɛ wɔnnye wɔn kɔɔ so ɛna wɔresɛe amanyɔkuo a ɔwɔ ɔmantam mu mpaninfoɔ a wɔfrɛ no IFP firi local councilor.
“Nhyiamu a wɔda IFP yi ano wɔ King Cetshwayo mantam mu sɛ ɔde ɔteɛ asɛm yi a ɛdi nnipa dodoɔ yi aturuturasɛm a ɛbuee mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a yɛfrɛ no Bonginkosi Biyela.
Wɔn a ɔmanfoɔ biara nnipa a wɔwɔ kwantempɔn so bere a wɔtoo tuo no, a na ɔmpɛ sɛ wɔnyɛ wɔn din no, ɔka kyerɛɛ IFP mpaninfoɔ ne ahemfo a wɔhwɛ wɔn so sɛ wɔnnye wɔn ani nto mu sɛ wɔmmɔ wɔn bo ase.
"Na yɛrekasa wɔ kwan no so esiane sɛ yɛma wɔn mmra hall no firisɛ nnipa a wɔte saa firisɛ amanfoɔ biara.
Ɔhaw no hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a yɛhunuu sɛ ɔde bɛsɔɔ ɔmanfoɔ foforɔ bi a wabu wɔn kwan mu ne banbɔfoɔ ne ahemfo a wɔhwɛ ma wɔn no shoot.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔda IFP taa di Mthonjaneni ano, a na ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ wɔn na wɔnmboa wɔn ho.
Nnawɔtwe a ɛwa mu no, na ɛrekasa akyerɛ wɔn a ɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ma wɔn aban apa wɔn mansini no so.
Nhyiamu a ɛhyɛɛ aseɛ nhyiamu a wɔne akuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ mantam mu ntam sɛ wɔn nteeɛ ma ɔmanfoɔ.
"Ɔhaw no hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a ɔmanfoɔ bi hyɛn aseɛ wɔ hall no mu, na berɛ a nhyiamu ahyɛ aseɛ no, wɔbɔɔ hall no mu, na wɔtwe ntoasoɔ bi a ɔde bɔ hall no ho nti, wɔhyɛɛ wɔn aseɛ sɛ ɔmanfoɔ no nso reko atia wɔn.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, "wɔakyɛfoɔ biara wɔbɔ wɔn a wɔde sika hyɛ nnwuma mu.
Ná nhyiamu yi nisuo abatoɔ Mbangiseni Biyela, ne deputy Phumlani Ntombela ne nnipa dodoɔ a ɔthonee Mthonjaneni mansini no anim.
Ɔtempae sɛ wɔbɛka asɛm a ɛfiri mantam no ankɔsi wɔn dwumadie no mu, nanso ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn space callsɛm akɔhwɛ na wɔn mm message no antwerɛ.
Sammɔntuo panin a ɔwɔ mansini no Thami Shangase se, ɔkaa sɛ nhyiamu yi nnipakan anim no planned, adding thatɛ asɛm no wɔ polisi so.
Ɔkɔɔ so ne IFP panin a ɔwɔ hɔ Mkhuleko Hlengwa kaa sɛ amanyɔkuo no bɛtɔ asɛm no ho nsɛm nnɛ.
Violence began with the dismissal of Biyela (former mayor) ne four councilors mu, na ɛde nnipa a ɔwɔ kyɛfa wɔ mansini no mu ntam, ne deɛ nnipa dodoɔ bi a wɔyɛ IFP wɔ charge wɔ mansini no mu.
KwaZulu-Natal polisifoɔ Colonel Thembeka Mbele kaa sɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛsɔ sɛ mmonnaa sɛ attempted murder ne akusere a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Melmoth polisi station no.
Mbete deniesɛm nnyinasoɔ biara
Mmarahyɛbɛdwa fie mu kasamafoɔ Baleka Mbethe asrɛ sɛ ɔreka nsɛm a ɛrekɔ so no yɛ asɛm bi.
Asɛnnibea bi a ɔhwehwɛ nsɛm a wɔde amanyɔsɛm ho nhwehwɛmu te sɛ nnipa bi wɔn nnyinasoɔ a wɔwɔ kyɛfa wɔ amanyɔsɛm ho na wɔgu so sɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ kyɛfa wɔ amanyɔsɛm ho nso na biom nso ɛte sɛ nnipa bi wɔn nnyinasoɔ corruption.
Ɔsan de ɔkwan a ɔde reko atia ɔmanpanin a watwam, Jacob Zuma kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɔma wɔn nsɛm bi ntɛm nanso ɔnkae sɛ ɔne no yɛɛ ɔbarima bi.
“Ɔpanin, mennim sɛ abɛdiakyire a wɔteteɛ ha abɛɛfo kwan sɛ ɔman no mu nnipa annyɛ adwuma.
Minim sɛ asɛm no ase abɔ ha na ɔka sɛ woayɛ biribiara a ɛnsɛ sɛ woreka no ntɛm.
M'ani nna asɛm no ho asɛm, ɛyɛ mmara ketewaa a asɛm no ase Benada (Monday).
krataa bi a wɔde krataa firii me office no so.
krataa a krataa no kyerɛɛ wɔn a ɛyɛ nsunsuanso, na ɛsɛ sɛ krataa no ankasa nkyerɛ wɔn, nanso obiara ntena na ɔtwe nsɛm no.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no ayɛ bebree, na mitumi nkyerɛw saa nhoma no a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔnkae nea ɔkyerɛw no na yɛkɔfaa ne ho asɛm.
Ɔhaw no nea ɔkyerɛkyerɛwfo no, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔbaa saa na ɔne me nyɛɛ adwene.
Mbete ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ wɔn mma wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu no yɛbɛkɔ sɛ wɔn mma wɔn nkasa nkitahodie,"
Wɔ afe 2017 mu no, wɔbɔɔ nea na ɔreyɛ wɔ asɛm bi a ɛda Indiaman no ho asɛm a ɛwɔ asɛm no mu.
M'atipɛnfo de too dwa,"mekae sɛ na ɛkae asɛm a ɛda nsɛm a ɛrekɔ so affecting the Guptas no.
Misusuw sɛ bere a saa nsɛm yi baakyere no, yɛbɛhwehwɛ those a ɔkyerɛw wɔn no so.
Ma yɛnhu nea wɔsɛ sɛ woka nsɛm wɔ wiase ase.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, “Sɛ yɛma yɛkyerɛkyerɛ nhwehwɛmu na yɛatumi ayɛ yɛn adwuma,”
Wɔbɔɔ NSFAS ama kuo bi a na wɔwuu adesuafoɔ
ƆUDENTSfoɔ no bɔɔ NSFAS aba so sɛ akuma abɔdin bi a na ɔwɔ sukuu no dan mu a wadi mfeɛ aduanan nnwɔtwe nsia awu wɔ ayaresabea, Durban Tvet College, a ɛwɔ Cato Manor no Memenda.
kyerɛ sɛ wawu no, nea wawu no yɛ ababaawa a yɛfrɛ no Electrical Infrastructure Construction, na ɔno nso yɛ ɔnwabo Manyanya (26), a ɔyɛ Electrical Infrastructure Construction adwuma no ma rentɔ arrears.
Ɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛn ntade mmienu no ankyɛn wɔ baabi a ɔwɔ kyɛfɛ no, efisɛ na ɔno ankasa biara mfi ne kyɛfɛ a na ɔwɔ fie no Dwoada no.
Wukuada no amaneɛ sɛ na awu no nyɛ apɔwmuden.
Asoafoɔ no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ obetumi hia baabi foforo.
Wɔka sɛ osuahunu a ɔte asubɔnten no, na ɔka kyerɛ sɛ wanya ne mpena a na ne mpena no yɛ flat a ɔda ne yere na ɔte Durban North.
Adesuafoɔ a wɔde awu no, a na ɔno nso yɛ wɔn kaa no, a ɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ ɛyɛɛ nea na asɛm no siiɛ wɔn, na ɔkaa sɛ NSFAS ntumi ɛna wɔn ka yie wɔn sika ho.
"Mepɛ me ho hwee bere a asɛm a anigye wɔ saa dwumadie yi ho no.
Mepɛ sɛ NSFAS adwene nhyɛ sɛ ɔwɔ sini sɛ ɛbɛyɛ asɛm a ɛwɔ awia yi, berɛ a awɔ a ɛsii wɔ awia mu no,”said adesuafoɔ no.
abusua baako a wawu no wɔ hɔ a wɔn ani nnye no kae sɛ wɔn nsɛm nsɛm yi nkɔmɔ.
KwaZulu-Natal polisifoɔ panin, Captain Nqobile Gwala kaa sɛ asɛm biara nni sɛ ɔbɛyɛ biara.
Sikasɛm ntotoeɛ a ɛwɔ Aserville Sukuu no ntam faako a ɛwɔ Sydenham no sɛ adesuafoɔ bɛyɛ 50 na ɔka kyerɛɛ adesuafoɔ a wɔwɔ n’asɛm no mu outside the gates no so.
Asuafoɔ no ka kyerɛɛ Isolezwe sɛ wobetumi awofoɔ hyɛn a ɛda hɔ no nti evicted from wɔn a wɔsom bosea no nsakraeɛ.
Adesuafoɔ a wɔwɔ pajamas no mu a na wɔne wɔn a wohiaa ɔte Gauteng, Eastern Cape ne Mpumalanga.
Owura Siyabonga Sambu a ɔfrɛɛ Ermelo, Mpumalanga a ɔyɛ Community Safety degree student, ka kyerɛɛ adwumayɛfoɔ no sɛ wasan no ne NSFAS fata wɔn ho bere a wɔhwehwɛ wɔn sika ho ase.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛfeɛkuu afe yi wɔnnyaa aban biara nti adesuafoɔ no guu adesuafoɔ a wɔmfa Kwan mu.
"Mo sika mma aduan.
Wɔmaa ntwaafo no ma wɔde transportation costs, na wɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnnyaa mmiɛnsa.
Sambu de ɔkwan no so yɛ deɛ ɛnnyɛ ɛna ɔka guardfoɔ no sɛ ɔvict yɛn,”
Yei yɛɛ Zodwa Mabanga a ɔte Johannesburg kyerɛɛ mu sɛ na ɔreyɛ asɛm yi mu firisɛ ɔbɔɔ no tena evicted.
Dr Mthabisi Bhebhe, panin paa a ɔwɔ Mpilo Hospital Doctors Association no kaa sɛ n’ani gye na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ Dr. Magombeyi adi kan kɔɔ mu sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ alive. Dr Bhebhe a ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association na ɔkaa sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔwɔ nsɛm no kɔɔ mu.
Dr. Tawanda Manjonjo a ɔyɛ dɔkotafoɔ a wadwene sɛ ɔfrɛ no Dr. Magombeyi hɔ maa dɔkotafoɔ no nsii gyinae sɛ ɔde ne ho ahyɛ n'anim. Nanso ɔka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ, sɛ ɔdɔkotafoɔ no mmere no a, ɔrenkɔ adwuma ntɛm.
Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ panin a ɔda Mpilo ayaresabea no ano, Leonard Mabandi kaa sɛ, nea ɔnim no, dɔkotafoɔ a wɔyɛɛ adwuma no hyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔbɛkɔ adwuma ntɛm ara.
Ɔbarima bi a ɔte ne din sɛ Walter, a ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ dɔkotafoɔ abɛhia ne yere treated no, seesei abɔdeɛ mu dɔkotafoɔ nnyɛ wɔn.
Doctorfoɔ redi atuateɛ berɛ a na Doctor Magombeyi abducted. Dɔkotafoɔ redi atuateɛ nnawɔtwe mmienu no se wɔbɛwie awieɛ sɛ wɔn ntumi nyɛ transportation.
Aban no se ɔreyɛ mmara sɛ ɛbɛma dɔkotafoɔ nsɛm afa wɔn ho ban, nanso adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ kyerɛ sɛ, ɛyɛ unkonstitutional.
Nnipa bebree de kɔkɔɔ bebree ase bɛtɔɔ Kentucky ahempɛn a ɛwɔ United States no bidumi ato Muhammad Ali a wadi mfeɛ aduonu nsia kɔɔ so afe a atwam no aduowɔtwe wadi mfeɛ ahanu.
Nnipa foforɔ a wɔne wɔn a yɛne wɔ dan mu no ne US Ɔmanpanin Bill Clinton, abaduaba a wɔfrɛ no George Foreman, Mike Tyson ne Lenox Lewis ne Will Smith, a well-known film star.
Ɔmanpanin Obama de n'ani atwitwa asɛm mu. Zimbabwe bi a ɔwɔ Louisville, Kentucky, Patricia Chikanga se ɔman no betumi ama ɔkwan biara a atwa yɛn ho ahyia a ɔbɛyi wɔn a wawu wɔn no ho.
“Manya no nteeɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔbɔɔ ɔman no mu bi maa wɔn awu te sɛ Muhammad Ali atwa yɛn ho sɛnea yɛhwɛ maa wɔn yi ase. yɛ da a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ kurow no mu ne nkurɔfo a wɔhwɛ maa wɔn a wɔbɔɔ ɔman no mu ayɛ adwuma. Yei hyɛɛ me da sɛ m’ani gye paa sɛ ɛbɛyɛ yɛn maa wɔn a wɔbɔɔɔ ɔman no mu bio.”Ms Chikanga ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7.
Ekuo a ɛhwɛ nkunimdifoɔ wɔ Zimbabwe Council of Churches (ZCC) se ɛyɛ nwanwa wɔ Matabeleland South, Matabeleland North ne Bulawayo mansini no mu sɛ wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛma nkurɔfoɔ a wɔyɛ nnwuma wɔ ayaresabea nnwuma mu wɔ mantam no mu.
ZCC akɔgye protective clothing to donateɛ, dɔkotafoɔ ne adekyerɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ dɔkotafoɔ wɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ wɔ mansini no mu.
ZCC panin paa, Pastor Doctor Kenneth Mtata ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ wɔn ahu sɛ nnipa pii a wɔn nnwɔtwe na ɛhaw no ase.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ne nsa asɔe no firi torture mu, na ɔka kyerɛɛ sɛ ne nsa asɔe no firi torture mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ aban no hwehwɛ amanyɔsɛm mu na ntɛm ara nsi wɔn a ɔbɛboa nnipa a wɔn di sɔree ara no.
Dr Mtata kaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛeɛ no bɛma aban no ahu ɛnsɛm nyinaa ara sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛma asuafoɔ anya aduan na ɛde ansa na wɔn bo afuw.
Zimbabwe sika kɔkɔɔ so wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduanan nnwɔtwe kɔ so wɔ afe 2007 ne 2008.
Amerika sika kɔkɔɔ de wɔn dɔla aduonu num.

Nanso Professor Mugano se n’ahwɛsofoɔ biara nni hɔ a ɔmma ɔman no dɔm no ɔhyɛ karrier mu efisɛ ɔman no aban abɔ nsam no ntumi ɔman no dɔm.

Nanso RBZ aban panin, Dr John Mangudya se, saa na ɛyɛ a ɔreka.

Nanso ɔtetena a ɔte Zimbabwefoɔ Nyasha Mahwende kaa sɛ, wɔn nyinaa yɛ wɔn yɛ adwuma sɛ wɔwɔ Zimbabwefoɔ ne wɔn nnamfoɔ ne wɔn nnamfoɔ.
Wɔkaa sɛ wɔn a yareɛ yareɛ no ara ne sɛ yareɛ yareɛ no ara nso te sɛ nnipa bi wɔn ho kwan sɛ wɔnfa nnipa bi ho ban na wɔasiesie wɔn sɛ wɔyɛ nnipa bi na wɔasiesie wɔn sɛ wɔn banbɔ yɛ banbɔ ho ban.
Banbɔfoɔ a wɔhwɛ Midlands Mantam mu ha adwene a ɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔn nni dwuma wɔ studio 7 ase ho.
Yɛtee sɛ nea ɔne Midlands Soafoɔ Larry Mavima ne a yɛfrɛ no provincial medical director Dr Reginald Mhene nanso yɛbaa ne n’abɛdiakyire no na ɔka sɛ ɔne wɔn nhyiamu biara.
Animdefoɔ kyerɛ sɛ wɔn kae sɛ, wɔ Botswana ne South Africa beaeɛ a wosusu sɛ nnipa a wodi wɔn yɛ adwuma no wɔ kwan bi so no, ɛno na ɛma wɔn yareɛ coronavirus.
Gweru manpanin Josiah Makombe a ɔwɔ VOA Studio 7 a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe bɔeɛ sɛ coronavirus anaa Isolation District Hospital no still under construction.
Ɔhyɛɛ aborofoɔ sɛ wɔn adwene nhyia wɔ ahyehyɛe a ɛbɛma wɔanya yareɛ coronavirus nkitahodie mu nanso ɔka sɛ wɔn nyɛ ho sɛ wɔbɛgye wɔn a wɔhwehwɛ virus no mu.
Amammuifoɔ panin, Lucia Matibenga a ɔte Gweru no yɛ mansini a ɔte saa no kaa sɛ ɛyɛ aban n'asoeɛ sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ amammuifoɔ a ɔwɔ fie na ɔbɛhwɛ amanfoɔ nyinaa ara.
Atɔeɛ mantam no mu biako a ɛwɔ afiri a atɔeɛ mantam no mu no ama Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔte fi atɔeɛ mantam no mu nti ɛma ebia ɔbɛyɛ wɔn head sɛ watumi atɔeɛ no.
Wukuada a ɔmanpanin dwumadibea hyɛɛ nhyiamu aseɛ wɔ Dɔkotafoɔ a wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu no Ɔbɛnem 1 a atwam no mu no.
Dɔkotafoɔ a watwa mu ne dɔkotafoɔ a ɔhwehwɛ nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ, Registrars ne Consultants nso aka wɔn ate atua Wukuada. Nnipa pii wɔ ɔman no mu se nkurɔfoɔ redi dɔkotafoɔ ahwehwɛ wɔn akwaa bi.
Ɔmanpanin a yɛfrɛ no Emmerson Mnangagwa kɔɔ holiday Benada no sɛ ɔne ne predecessor, General Constantino Chiwenga bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛmia ɔdɔkotafoɔ no gyinaeɛ ahodoɔ.
Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔfrɛ no Nick Mangwana kaa sɛ ɔgye di sɛ Mnangagwa a wakɔ adwumam no ayɛ adwuma de agu akɔneabadie no mu.
Benada no, Owura Chiwenga abɔ adwumayɛfoɔ kɛkɛ sɛ adwumayɛfoɔ return kɔ adwuma.
Senior dɔkotafoɔ a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe Medical Association ama aban no dɔkotafoɔ 48 hours sɛ wɔbɛhwehwɛ ɔhaw a ɛda dɔkotafoɔ nnwuma mu na wɔtɔ strike.
Nanso Mnangagwa adwumakuo no kɔɔ ɔne Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association panin, Dr Elias Muzoremba, sɛ wɔn nso oyia dɔkotafoɔsɛm yi ano.
Wɔ krataa a ɔkyerɛɛ nsɛm mu no, dɔkotafoɔ no ka kyerɛɛ Ɔmanpanin adwuma no sɛ wɔnnyae sɛ Apɔmuden Asoeɛ no mbɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔnnye apɔmuden.
Dɔkotafoɔ no se wɔpɛ sɛ aban yɛ hwehwɛ ɔhaw a ɛda ayaresabea ne ayaresabea nnwuma mu na wɔde wɔn US dollar wɔ ɛkwan a wɔde ma ɛdaadaa ɛntanɛt so.
Dɔkotafoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman yi mu no, wɔde dɔkotafoɔ bɛyɛ ɔpepem 329 a ɛwɔ RTGS.
Nanso sikasɛm ne nnwuma mu adesuafoɔ bi a ɔwɔ Nelson Mandela Metropolitan University, Professor Gift Mugano ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ aban no ntumi mma no nyɛ sika no ara.
Yɛsan bisaa Dr Mugano sɛ, nneɛma bi wɔ hɔ a nnwuma no, US dollar bɛko ama wɔn nnwuma no, ɛyɛ dɛn na wɔatumi ayɛ?
Otitenani a ɔtua Community Working Group on Health ano, Owura Itai Rusike ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛho abɛhia sɛ aban bɛma apɔmuden nnwuma no sika pii wɔ ɔsram no mu.
Nnipa pii wɔ ɔman no mu nso rehu sɛ Apɔmuden Asoeɛ cards nnyɛ workingna ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde US dollar bɛba fie mpo a, na wɔreka akyerɛ wɔn sɛ ɔde ɔbaa US dollar bɛba fie mpo.
Warriors akorɔmfoɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo no akɔ South Africa kwan wɔ Cosafa toɔ no mu.
Kuo no akansiesie wɔn akansie wɔ Cosafa Cup ne Africa Cup a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn bɛkuo no nkunim berɛ a na wɔn akansiesie wɔn ho berɛ a na wɔyɛɛ Cosafa Cup a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Memeneda no.
Bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtoaa Cosafa Cup wɔ Afcon no mu a, ɛsɛ sɛ Zimbabwe bɛhyɛ bɔɔlobɔ kurow a ɛtɔ so nsia awieɛ no, a ɛtɔ so aduonu nson na wɔhyɛɛ bɔɔlobɔ afe yi mu. Wɔpɛ sɛ Zimbabwe bɛhyɛ bɔɔlobɔ kurow a ɛtɔ so nsia awadeɛ wɔ afe yi mu, na wɔbɛhyɛ bɔɔlbɔ kurow a wɔyɛ North African football champion afe yi mu.
nam so sika a ɛwɔ mu no, Zimbabwe ntumi nyin nea wɔbɛyɛ teams bɛkɔɔ afcon akansie no mu, na ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ Sunday Chidzambwa se, Saa ara na ɛkyerɛ sɛ Cosafa yɛ ɛkwan ne squad no.
Chidzambwa nso dii n’ani gu so wɔ Cosafa akansie no mu berɛ a onyɛ ɔkoo a ɔdi kan wɔ akansie no mu mmiɛnsa a ɛdi kan no wɔ 1997.
Chidzambwa bɔɔ Cosafa Cup wɔ 2003, 2009, 2017 ne 2018.
Other Zimbabwean bɔɔlbɔkuo bi te sɛ Tendai Darikwa, Admiral Muskwe ne Alec Mudimu nso pɛ sɛ wɔn appear wɔ Cosafa Cup a ɛwa wɔn ho ahyia.
Nsusueɛ afe yi mu no, Zimbabwefoɔ no wɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo panin wɔ akansie no mu a ɛresɛe wɔn a wɔyɛɛ mmɔden wɔ Afcon, a wɔne mmɔden bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu te sɛ Knowledge Musona ne Marvelous Nakamba.
Wɔn a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Warriors Fan Club, Shingirai Miti se nkɔmmɔ biara nni ho sɛ Cosafa tiri no Zimbabwean ɛfiri.
Having won the Cosafa Cup no mu no, the Warriors no rennye ho kwan a ɛdi kan ahyɛ wɔ Afcon akansie aseɛ a ɛdaa na wɔhyiaa Egypt wɔ akansie a ɛtɔ so awieɛ no.
Kual no bɔɔlbɔni a yɛfrɛ no, Ronald Pfumbidzai se wɔn ntumi nkɔ Egypt sɛ wɔn bɛka bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu.
Wɔ Aman, Egypt, the Democratic Republic of Congo ne Uganda a ɛwɔ Sikasɛm ho nhyehyɛeɛ no, wotukuw a yɛfrɛ no Wellington Mpandare gyee ne ho sɛ ɔbɛtu anɔpa.
Wɔbɛyi mmerɛ South Africa wɔ akuo ahodoɔ a ɛdi kan wɔ Cosafa akansie yi mu Ayɛwohomumɔ 8, 2017, wɔ Nigeria bɛkɔɔ the Afcon wɔ Egypt.
Wɔn a wɔyɛ atɔeɛfoɔ no pii no, Christmas holiday season yɛ bere a wɔn nnamfo ne nnamfo bɔ wɔn ho. Afe yi yɛ bere a mmusuakuw bi na wɔn nnamfo ne nnamfo bɔ wɔn ho. Nanso afe yi ara yɛ bere a wɔn na wɔn nnamfo ne nnamfo bɔ wɔn ho. FC Platinum coach Lizwe Sweswe ne ne n’abusua team no ntumi nnyaa wɔn kwan bi so wɔ Cairo, Egypt, berɛ a wɔhyɛɛ Al Ahly wɔ Caf Champions League no mu.
Yei bɛyɛ FC Platinum akansie a ɛtɔ so aduonu wɔ akansie yi mu berɛ a na Sudan's Al Hilal dii kan wɔ akansie a ɛdi kan no, losing 3-0 to Tunisia's Etoile duSahel.
Sweswe se wɔn bɛbɔ nkɔmmɔ a wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtwe wɔn nhyehyɛeɛ no mu bɛka sɛ wonnii wɔn ani na wɔnhwɛ no so. Another football soɔ, Darlington Dodo of Caps United se aberɛ a wɔn ntumi mmienu yi wɔn sika kɔkɔɔ Premier Soccer League trophyi mu a wɔn ani ayɛ basaa. Nanso ɔbaa ne mmonnaa a ɔda Zimbabwe Olympic Committee ano, Anna Mguni kaa sɛ wɔkɔ wɔn fie hɔ maa nkurɔfo ne nnamfo a ɔte nka sɛ wabra wɔn ntam.
Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a ɛwɔ Akwan (ARTUZ) se Ɔman no mu asɛm sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔwɔ ɔhaw no gyinaberɛ mu dapɛn 14, a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔtoteɛ no.
Ekuo no se wɔpɛ sɛ wɔbɛgyaa akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ nnwuma wɔ US dollars, anaa wɔbɛgyaa wɔn dɔla ahasa.
Nteeɛ kyerɛɛ wɔn a aban firi civil service, Public Service Commission ne Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Sikasɛm mu ntotoeɛ.
Studio7 annye n’adwene sɛ aban ka ho asɛm wɔ asɛm yi ho, berɛ a Ɔsoafoɔ Panin Monica Mutsvangwa n’adwene nhyia wɔ ne telefon so.
ARTUZ panin, Obert Masaraure se asɛmtiafoɔ no bi nso ahia sɛ, wɔn pɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ a ɛbɛma wɔabɛse pa ara, nanso ɛrentumi nni saa.
Masaraure se ɛwɔ sɛ aban no reka ɔhaw wɔ sikasɛm ne nnwuma mu ntotoeɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛbɛboa nnipa dodoɔ a ɔman no sikasɛm ne nnwuma mu nsakraeɛ.
Masaraure se aban sika no yɛ deɛ wɔn sika kɔkɔɔ wɔ nsɛm ho nimdeɛ bi te sɛ amamfra trips, kar insurance ne nneɛma bi a ɛbɛtumi asɛe wɔn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ama aban nnwuma a ɔbɛhwɛ ama adwumayɛfoɔ.
Masaraure se wɔ nea ɔkyerɛ mu no, sika wɔ ɔman yi mu a wɔbɛtumi ayɛ ɔhaw no mu, nanso ɔhaw no yɛ sɛ ɔman no treasury no being managed properly, na wɔn nnyɛ hwee sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ nneɛma a ɛfa aban mu firi hɔ.
Nnwumakuw a wɔkɔɔ ɔmanfoɔ foforɔ no rehwehwɛ wɔn kwan a ehia sɛ wɔbɛgu akwan foforɔ anaa wɔn ahyɛ aseɛ foforɔ.
Yei hyɛɛ aban nkra a wɔde too dwa Dwoada da a ɛtɔ so mmeɛnsa yi ase sɛ wɔmfa Zimbabwefoɔ ɔpepepem ɔha aduoson ($ 388 million).
Ɔrekasa akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ no, Asoeɛ a ɔhwɛ nnipa-kɔɔ so no Kazembe kaa sɛ n’abɛhia sɛ nnipa a wɔn ho nsɛm yiyɛ wɔn passport asɛm biara ntɛm paa ara, na nnipa a wɔn ntɛm paa ara ne wɔn a wɔn ntɛm nsii nsii.
Kazembe kaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ ahwɛ sɛ amamfrafoɔ no nyɛ mmara kwan wɔ wɔn home countries mu a, ɔman no aban anwene sɛ ɔbɛyɛ ɛtoɔ boɔ so, na ɛbɛsan de saa nkitahodie yi ara agu.
Nanso amanfoɔ pii nka sɛ aban de asi nnɔn so sɛ ɔhwehwɛ ɔman foforo so mma wɔn.
Ɔman bi a wɔfrɛ no RTGS wɔ ɔman no mu no, egyina ɔpepem aduonu num. Deɛ ɔpɛ sɛ wɔn mma wɔn mma $ 53, na wɔn baako a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔn mma wɔn mma $ 250.
sɛ sɛ wɔkyere passport issued within ɔpepem baako akyire no, boɔ yɛ Dɔla a ɛboro ɔpepem 380.
Ekuo a ɛhwɛ ama mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu abɛdiakyire, Kindness Paradza kaa sɛ n’abɛdiakyire no sii gyinaeɛ a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔn mfa passport fees ɛboɔ ma wɔmfa nnipa ho nsɛm wɔ wɔn firi wɔn nsawɔsoɔ ho, na ama wɔn anya akwankyerɛ wɔ wɔn firi wɔn nsawɔsoɔ ho.

Haruzivishe kaa sɛ bere a yɛtu nsɛm no kɔɔ akyi no wɔ asɛm no mu na wɔn nhwehwɛ polisifoɔ nhwehwɛmu wɔ saa asɛm yi ho, nanso kaa sɛ wɔn aware baako.

Aban nso kaa sɛ ɛnyɛ mmofra a wɔkɔ polisifoɔ yi ase firisɛ wɔde akɔ kɔɔto akɔkyere wɔn a wɔbɛto polisifoɔ yi ama wɔn.
Yɛnntumi nnyaa asɛm yi ho mmuae apolisifoɔ.
Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa, ankorɛankorɛ bi wɔ South Africa, seesei nnyɛ Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔdii sika wɔ Johannesburg akɔbɔ mu a akorɔmfoɔ bi nom seesei Zimbabwefoɔ agyae.
Kuo no se nkɔmmɔ no nnipa pii wɔ Hillbrow, Berea ne Yeoville hɔ ma amanfoɔ a wɔyɛ Zimbabwefoɔ nhwehwɛmu. Kuo no se nnipa pii wɔ hɔ a wɔsusu sɛ wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu, ahemfoɔ wɔ hɔ, akyiri kɔkɔɔ ne mmienu a wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu.
Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa ano kwankyerɛfoɔ Bongani Mkwananzi kaa sɛ wɔnhyɛ apolisifoɔ no sɛ wɔnmuo asɛm no ho mmuaeɛ, na wɔnhyɛ polisifo no sɛ wɔnnye mma asɛm no ho yiye.
Ɔkaaeɛ afe 6, a ɛkɔɔ so no, n’adwumayɛfoɔ no daa adi sɛ ɔne polisifoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu sɛ ɔne wɔn bɛtumi ayɛ adwuma ama ɔhaw no ho mmuaeɛ.
Wɔsan nso ka sɛ apolisifoɔ should bekosi wɔn paa ho, nanso ɛnte saa ara na korɔnobɔfoɔ dodoɔ a ɔyɛ robɔt ne akorɔmfoɔ a wɔdii Jojina bidding.
Owura Mkwananzi kaa sɛ akurɔfoɔ a wɔn a wɔdii sa abɔ wɔn yi nyinaa nimdeɛ abɔ mu nnipa bi wɔ wɔn mu so nti polisifoɔ a wɔn committed to the crime should be working with Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔwɔ saa mansini yi mu.

Ɔkaa asɛm yi a ɔde maa Ghana Sikasɛm Soafoɔ, Owura Ken Ofori-Attah hyɛɛ no bɛboa ɔmanfoɔ a wanya nsunsuansoɔ a ɔde rehwehwɛ nsɛm a ɛho hia nwanwa bi a wɔyɛ manpanin a wɔne ɔmanpanin anantew no ho.
“Manyaa asɛm yi adi sɛ ɛbɛba saa ɔman yi mu wɔ 2013 kɔɔ so aberɛ a Ɔmanpanin Mahama dii dwumadie a ɔkɔɔ so wɔ ɛne akwantuo a wɔyɛɛ ho akwantuo no ho”
ɛnyɛ equalisation mma obiara.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ ɔrebɛkyerɛ asɛm no a ɛsii wɔ dan no mu a Owura Barimah kaa sɛ n’asɛm no nyɛ amanyɔsɛm.
“Yei ka ankasa yɛɛn nhyehyɛeɛ sɛ yɛbɛyɛ ɔman yi manfoɔ wɔ akwantuo a ɛwɔ mu dabiara ɛne yɛhunuu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛhunu sɛnea wɔyɛ biara no.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Yei yɛ precedence? Sɛ ebia ɛkɔɔ so a, nea edidi so yi yɛ baako anaa? Nneɛma a ɛho hia paa wɔ aban keteke kwan a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ amanyɔsɛm mu akɔyɛ adwuma? Yei nti, mempɛ sɛ wɔnyɛ amanyɔsɛm mu amanyɔsɛm akɔyɛ adwuma.”
Ɔkaa sɛ: “Mepɛ sɛ yɛn anya asɛm ne discourse sɛnea yɛbɛhwɛ ama yɛn anya nteaseɛ ma yɛn. Nnɛ, ebia me aban nanso ɛbɛyɛ obiara sɛ ɔbɛkyerɛ ma yɛn, enti sɛ yɛn hwehwɛ nteaseɛ ma yɛn anya nsɛm pa a, ɛbɛduru kwan na yɛbɛduru kwan”
Ablakwa asɛm no ho mmuae
Ranking Member a ɔhwɛ Sikasɛm Soafoɔ abɛdiakyire, Owura Samuel Okudzeto Ablakwa nso de asɛm a ɛsɛ sɛ aban no kyerɛ nea enti a Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo adi kɔɔ so wɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu sɛ ɔne Ɔmanpanin nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo adi n’ani nnyɛ presidential kwan wuranom berɛ a ɛkɔɔ France.
National Democratic Congress (NDC) North Tongu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu kyerɛ sɛ, "Yei yɛ nneɛma ani na ɛrekɔ so sɛ Ghana bɔɔ presidential ahyɛn a wɔde reyɛ adwuma no wɔ akwan a atwa mu no" ne akwan a wɔhyɛn a wɔde reyɛ adwuma no wɔ berɛ mu.
Ɔsan nso estima sɛ Ɔmanpanin dwumadie no boɔ yɛ nea ɛboro GH¢2 million.
Bono East Mansini Soafoɔ, Owura Kwasi Adu-Gyan abɔ Mantam no amanyɔkuo New Patriotic Party ne National Democratic Congress (NDC) aba so wɔ ɔman no asomdwoeɛ wɔ ɔmantam no mu.
“Mepɛ sɛ NPP ne NDC a ɛwɔ Bono East working together peacefully, wɔ resolving amanyɔsɛm a ɛda wɔn ntam no mu”
Owura Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ asomdwoeɛ yi deɛ ɛbɛboa ama mpuntuo nkan ntumi nsawɔ wɔ ɔmantam no mu na ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ without asomdwoeɛ ɛbɛyɛ den ama mpuntuo nnwuma wɔ ɔmantam no mu.
Ɔman soafoɔ no de saa bɔɔ yi wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Techiman.
NPP ne NDC na nnipa a wɔayiyi wɔn ntam yi, abatoɔ asoeɛ, Ekuo a ɛhwɛ Apaadie so (EC) ne National Commission or Civic Education (NCCE) ne civil society organisations (CSOs) na wɔdii saa dwumadie yi.
National Peace Council dwumadie a ɔwɔ Commonwealth Secretariat na ɛhyɛɛ ɛtema: “Countering Post 2020 Abatoɔ Violence, ne Building Consensus for Greater Political Tolerance wɔ Ghana “
Abatoɔ asɛm no ho nsɛm a ehia de kasa wɔ abatoɔ asɛm no ho, na wɔde bɛsɔ abatoɔ asɛm no ho ayɛ den.
Owura Adu-Gyan kaaɛ sɛ Ghanafoɔ nni ho kwan sɛ ɔman no agye asomdwoeɛ a ɛto so peaceful wɔ Abibirem afe 2021 mu, na ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɛwɔ NPP ne NDC amammuo a wɔde boaa asomdwoeɛ na ɛbɛboa ama asomdwoeɛ a ɛbɛboa ama asomdwoeɛ wɔ ɔman yi mu.
“Yei yɛ ahenkuroɔ a ɛdi kan a ɛyi manfoɔ, ahemfoɔ a wɔhwɛ amanyɔkuo, banbɔ ne Judiciary ne Nsɛntwerɛfoɔ”
Ɔma ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ Regional Coordinating Council (RCC) no bɛboa ama asomdwoeɛ a ɛhia sɛ asomdwoeɛ a ɛbɛboa ama mpuntu dwumadie no mpuntuo nnya.
Wɔ berɛ a ɔne Electoral Justice rekasa no, Bono Regional Peace Council panin, Alhaji Suallah Abdallah Quandah kaa sɛ, anobaa a ɔwɔ ma amanyɔsɛm mu no yɛ ntɛm paa wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu yie paa wɔ ɔman no mu.
“Abatoɔ kɔmisa electoral justice ɛwɔ da foforɔ a ɛmu da hɔ no nyaa mmaa wɔn ho asɛm sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a abatoɔ kɔmisa mu dabiara wɔn ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a abatoɔ kɔmisa mu.”
Alhaji Quandah hyɛɛ ɔman yi abatoɔ asoeɛ pɛ ara sɛ ɔbɛyɛ biribi ama ɔman yi abatoɔ asoeɛ system no ahiadeɛ sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ama abatoɔ a ɛmu yɛ pɛ na amma abatoɔ akɔ so yie.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Abuakwa South Samuel Atta Akyea ahyɛ Ghanafoɔ sɛ Nana Akufo-Addo aban no bɛte wɔn ɔhaw fiti January 7, 2017.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, Ghanafoɔ bɛnya sikasɛm ahofadi under Nana Akuffo-Addo amammuo kyerɛ mu sɛ ɔbɛyɛ sikasɛm nsɛm a ɛbɛgu so.
“January 7 bɛyɛ eraan a ɛbɛma yɛn prosperity ne yɛn ɑhofama, ne titiriw ne sikasɛm a ɛyɛ Ghanafoɔ de srɛ. Afei nso, Ghanafoɔ behu sɛ God ama ayɛ ɔman no mu ayɛ mmerɛw” Atta Akyea kaa kyerɛɛ wɔ akayɛ a Asiakwa SOS wɔ East Akim mansini a ɛwɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu wɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu
Ɔkaa sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔbɛgyaa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ ama ɔmanpanin-elect Nana Akufo-Addo sɛ ɔbɛgyaa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ adi dwuma.
Nneɛma a ɔde kaa ho kyerɛɛ mu no bi ne nnuan a ɔde nsawɔtwe, nsukyenee, atosode, milk, drinks ne undisclosed amount of money.
Wɔkyeree nnipa mmienu a wɔatwa wɔn maame sɛ wɔwoo wɔn baabi a ɛwɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta a ɛwɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem mansini a ɛwɔ Atɔew Mantam mu
Nnipa baanan na wɔde generator bɔne no so abufuw.
Chief Inspector George Sekyi a ɔyɛ Tarkwa-Nsuta adwumayɛbea dwumadie kae sɛ, Ɔbɛnem 18, wɔfrɛɛ wɔnfrɛɛ wɔn wɔn so a mmofra nnipa baanu no awu wɔ baabi a na wɔn menea koraa.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɔkoyi ne n’asraafoɔ kɔɔ beaeɛ hɔ nanso wɔn ka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ Abena Amos, 15, Arabi Dadzi, 13 ne Akaba Dadzi, 7 na wɔde awu no wɔ Tarkwa Aban ayaresabea ayarehwɛ mu awaiting autopsy.
Wɔ Starr News anototoɔ mu no, Emmanuel Ohene Gyan Owura Sekyi kaa sɛ na wawu no ne wɔn maame, a ɔno nso yɛ adwuma “Golden City Kitchen” drinking spot a ɛwɔ Tarkwa Nsuem mansini mu.
Ɔkae sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wogyinae anadwo wɔ bar no so bere a na wɔaboa wɔn maame sɛ wɔverɛ nnua beverages no mu.
Asanteɛbea dwumadibea no kaa sɛ, Dɔɔtɔnima bosome a ɛtɔ so dunson wɔ December 17, no, esiane sɛ akasakasa a ɛtɔ so wɔ da no yiye nti, esiane sɛdeɛ maame Dadzi de generator apam wɔ barima no mu sɛ ɛbɛma nea wawu no ayɛ mmerɛw sɛnea wɔn na wɔakyere no. Ɔbaa maame twee no kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ ɔde wɔn awu amaneɛ mu aberɛ na ɔkɔɔ tɔɔɔ so anɔpa akyi no.
Wɔde sister a ɛfiri sɛ ɔbaa ne mpena no awu no resi rekɔ ayarehwɛ. Polisifoɔ a ɛwɔ area no reyɛ nhwehwɛmu.
John Mahama se ɔman panin a ɔda National Democratic Congress ano sɛ ɔbɛpɛ Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah yɛ menzgold adwumakuo no NAM 1, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛgye held up investment of adwadifoɔ a wɔde sika wɔn di dwuma wɔ December polls mu.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem a ɛwɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu no, Owura Mahama wondered why Akufo-Addo aban rennyɛ sɛ ɔmfa anigyeɛ ne nnipa NAM1 ho nsɛm na rather ɔde wɔn bo afuw a wɔresɛe wɔn ani.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ “Nea ɛwɔ NAM 1 bɛso na Akufo-Addo redi him? Dɛn nti na wobue apolisifoɔ sɛ wɔn mma wɔn ho adwuma a wɔnam 1 walks free”
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ n’aban a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔnam anigyeɛ ne nnamfoɔ a wɔhwɛ NAM1 ne directors mu na wɔnhwɛ ɔkwan bi so de retrieve sika no mu.
Circuit Court a ɛwɔ Accra preside a Her Honour Ellen Asamoah de too dwa September 7 adjourned the asɛm a ɔdaa nadi sɛ Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah (NAM1) has been adjourned to October 1, 2020.
Na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔman no gyinaeɛ bi a ɛtɔ so aduonu nson wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu wɔ Accra Circuit Court no.
Assistant Commisioner of Police (ASP) Sylvester Asare de too kɔɔto no anim sɛ ɔnhyɛ Asare kɔɔto no ma Court no sɛ ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔmfa nyinaa nni asɛm yi ne plea a wɔakyere no bɔ wɔn so.
Ayɛwohomumɔ 20, ASP Asare ka kyerɛɛ kɔɔto no sɛ, wɔn ani gye bere a wɔrebɛtuo asɛm no gyinaberɛ nkɔ asɛm no mu.
Ƹwɔ saa mpɛmpɛnsɛm yi mu no, ɔhyɛɛ kɔɔto kɔɔto no sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔmfa asɛm no ntɛm a, anka wɔbɛtumi akyerɛ kɔɔto no adwene sɛ wɔmfa asɛm no ntɛm.
Ɔkaa sɛ berɛ a wɔadwuma no ahyɛ aseɛ no, wɔn bɛkɔ so ntɛmntɛm a wɔaka no adi sɛ wɔmfa nnipa a wɔabɔ wɔn no ho nhwehwɛmu.
Nanso wɔ Dwoada no, Kɔɔto no anim no, kwaadubɔfoɔ prayɛ sɛ wɔmfa nhyehyɛeɛ ankɔsi aga na wɔgye too mu.
Kwaadubɔfoɔ a wɔabɔ no Nam 1 wɔ Kɔɔto no ho.
Circuit Court de ɛwoɔ too dwa Kɔtɔnima bosome a ɛtɔ so aduonu nsia wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
Na ɔmpaa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ mmiɛnsa ɛsiane ne mmɔdenbɔ ɔha aduonu nan ase. Aban abɔdeɛ n’ahoɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔde ɔbɛsɔ no so ntɛm.
Ɔsan nso nso de ɔbɛka kyerɛɛ apolisifoɔ wɔ Wukuada a ɛbɛyɛ dɔn ara nnɔnhwerew.
Nteeɛ kyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔbetumi afa mmara so yi, defrauding by false pretences, carrying on a deposit-taking nnwuma a ɛho nhia, sale of minerals without licence, unlawful deposit-taking ne sika laundering.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ sɛ wɔabɔ asɛm yi adi sika kɔkɔɔ bi a na wɔtɔ sika ɛsiane sika kɔkɔɔ aduasa nnwɔtwe (GH1.6 billion).
Nteeɛ a ɛte saa wɔ Okada dwumadie no so no brɛɛ ade a ɛrekɔ so no.
Polisifoɔ akyerɛ sɛ akwannya pii wɔ akwan, nsu, ne kwan a ɛfa so nsɛmsɛm a ɛfa akwan ho so a mototɔhyɛn ho.
Without any doubt, Okada a ɛwɔ sɛ ɔbɛbrɛ abasakɔnmu no da so ara retu anamɔn a ɔwɔ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ ama akɔ yɛn dwumadie.
Yɛasɛm biara atu mpɛn pii anya ɔka bi ho asɛm a ɛhaw yɛn.
Saa ɛkwɑn yi, ɔman yi yɛ ɔhaw a ɛfa akwan ne mototɔɔ ho ne tricycle ho, ne titiriw wɔn adwuma a ɛfa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ ne nsɛntwerɛfoɔ.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu wɔ afe 2012 no, wɔbɔ Akwan Atennaeɛ, 2012 (L.I. 2180) wɔ mmara ma wɔn mma wɔn ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛbɛma ɔman no akwan mu.
Nkaseɛbɔ ho nso a ɛka ho nhwɛsoɔ no, Regulation 128 under section one kɔɔ four (Legislative Instrument (L.I.) 2180) outlaws sɛ wogyina mototwa foforɔ a yɛfrɛ no ‘Okada’ ne tricycles ho kwan sɛ ɛnyɛ ma kwan ma courier ne delivery services. ɛno nso hyɛɛ nsɛnpɛnsɛn authority sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ mototwa kwan ma ɔde fare-paying dwuma.
Saa mmarahyɛbɛdwani yi nni ho kwan sɛ okada ne tricycle (pragya) have taken over the ɔman yi mu wɔ mmeaeɛ bebree.
Wɔ mfidie mu no, wotumi de ɔkada ne pragya bɛtumi atwa wɔn ho sɛ ɛbɛma wɔatɔ market, apɔmuden ne kurow mu nkurow a wɔyɛɛ mu, among mmeaeɛ beaeɛ a wɔbɛyɛ ho.
Mma wɔn a wɔtete nka sɛ wɔbɛka kar ahorow mu no, wɔtumi anya wɔn ti di dwuma yiye na wɔnam so de bike ho.
Nhyehyɛeɛ no nso betumi ama wɔn a wɔyɛ transportation akodeɛ sɛnea ɛyɛ den paa.
Yɛsan atu kwan because of the absence of anamɔntuo a ɛmu yɛ akwankyerɛ a wɔbɛfa so atu kwan no mu.
Nnipa pii abɔ wɔn a wɔwɔ akwan ne pragya efisɛ ɛboɔ a wɔde ma akwan ahodoɔ no nni mu, ne titire no nnyinasoɔ a wɔwɔ nkrataa no so.
Nkwankyerɛfoɔ a ɛwɔ akwan ne nkwanhyia a ɛfa Okada adwuma no ho no nsusuw ho.
Anokwa, akwannya bi a ɛwɔ Ghana Medical Association ne National Road Safety Authority abɔ wɔn banbɔ sɛ wɔreka akwan wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Eyi de ɔman no haw firi ɔman no nsuyiri.
Yei kyerɛ sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ mmara no banbɔ Ghanafoɔ a wɔde wɔn dwumadie kwan so na wɔanya adwuma ama Ghanafoɔ.
Yɛdwene de Daily Graphic anim no, yɛdwene sɛ ɔman no mu nyinaa asɛm mmara ho na ɔde nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛboa nnipa dodoɔ no ara ahyɛ aban mu de a ɔbɛdi dwuma asomdwoeɛ.
India deɛ, pragya bɛyɛ transport so nanso yɛte sɛ nea ɛwɔ Ghana.
Enti deɛ yɛbɛsua firi India na yɛde ama yɛn nhomasua foforɔ mu?
sɛ sɛ yɛma yehu sɛ, berɛ a ɛresɛe nnipa a yɛnya adwuma no, nkrataa adwuma ne dwumadie a okada ne tricycle dwumadie no se, ɛyɛ income a ɛbɛboa wɔn ne wɔn families.
Nanso seesei ara no, okadas ne pragyas no yɛ abɔdeɛ mu ɛna yɛn a Daily Graphic dii so kyerɛ sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde mmarahyɛbɛdwafie hyehwɛ lɔɔn no mu kena sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɔman no nni dwuma ɛsɛ sɛ wɔwɔ wɔn ho.
Sɛnea wɔreyɛ current mmara a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ wɔ saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi mu no, ɛbɛma wɔn nteteeɛ, biribiara a wɔde toto nneɛma bi te sɛ motocycle/motor tricycles asɛm ne nsiaho nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔde cater for accidents no behia.
Sɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ bɛseɛ yi a, ɛbɛyɛ mmerɛ ama Ghana Polisi Asoeɛ sɛ wɔmfa mototwa ne motor tricycle ho asɛm na ɛnyɛ wɔn a wɔfa motokwan bi so a wɔredi nneyɛeɛ ho.
Currently, Ghanafoɔ agye wɔn kwan wɔ akwansideɛ mmienu ne wɔn a wɔbɛfa so nneɛma wɔ transport so efisɛ wɔn advantages ne disadvantages.
Daily Graphic gyedi sɛ sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ yɛbɛdi ɔhaw wɔ yɛn akwan mu na yɛbɛsi yɛn lɔɔre Kwan mu a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ dede toto ɔhaw no ho dwuma biara ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ nhwehwɛmu dapɛn na yɛbɛsan de akɔ ɔhaw no ho dwuma biara.
Me nka sɛ da biara nni hɔ a ɛyɛ anigye wɔ me recent memory mu wɔ Ghana sen sɛ last Friday, the Green Ghana day.
Yei yɛ da a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛhyɛ yɛn sɛ yɛkɔ afiri dwuma.
Mfe aduonu (20) kɔɔ Ghana nyaeɛ, na mihui sɛ ɔhaw a yɛn man yi mu no firisɛ nea wɔyɛ Geography nhom no, na yei yɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛdi dwuma wɔ ama yɛn man yi ho a wɔyɛ biribi ama ɔman no atu mpɔn.
Nnipa nsakraeɛ a ɛmaa Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ nsaase ne fagudeɛtuo bɛma yɛn mpem aduasa nnwɔtwe na m’ani agye paa.
Ebetumi ayɛ sɛ Ghanafoɔ behu sɛ nneɛma bi a ɛhia sɛ yɛbɛhwɛ kwan sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛfrɛ Ghana.
Akwan pii wɔ ɔkwan a ɛfa so anyinungi, anyinungi a ɔda sukuu no nketewa, anyinungi a ɔda sukuu no nketewa anaa sukuufoɔ a ɔyɛ ɔhaw afanaa nyinaa ara na mɛka sɛ, adeɛ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛtɔ na yɛhaw yɛn suban, nsu a ɛredi Kɔtɔnima bosome wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu, na mɛka sɛ yɛyɛ ɔhaw a ɛsɛ yɛn suban na yɛyɛ ɔhaw a ɛyɛ Kɔtɔnima bosome wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
M’adwene mpɛn pii wɔ sukuu dan mu a ɛrenyɛ Geography nhoma a ɛrenyɛ wɔ yɛn sukuu mu nnɛ, nanso misu sɛ ɛwɔ sɛnea Ghana nhoma a wɔwoo sukuu mu wɔ nhoma mu no nni ho sɛ ɛyɛ daa Ghana saa da.
Yɛbɛka ara sɛ yɛbɛyɛ afoforɔ kɛseɛ, nanso ɛnyɛ yɛn man no reality.
Yɛbɛka asoe koraa akyi nanso wɔde wɔn abɔ mu ɔhaw bi pɛ nanso wɔn habitat no ayɛ kɔpem akyi.
Mprɛ bebree a atwa yɛn mu no, abɔde a ɛte saa nnɛ nyinaa, na mmom abɔde a ɛte saa nnyɛ yɛn reality.
Na ehu sɛ ɛbɛyɛ nea yɛdwene sɛ wɔde sika kɔkɔɔ ne nsamhoɔ a ɛmu yɛ duru nhwehwɛmu.
Ebia ɛbɛma yɛn reality ɛka nea ɛsɛ sɛ yɛaka afiri ɔhaw bi mu, na mehwɛ sɛ wɔn a woaka afiri no nyɛ adwene bi a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ saa.
